
  

   Mfwwd Utyyjw fsi ymj Xtwhjwjw'x Xytsj

   Fsi ktw In, bmt mjfwi ymnx tsj knwxy.
  
  

   

    1. YMJ GTD BMT QNAJI
   

   Rw. fsi Rwx. Izwxqjd, tk szrgjw ktzw, Uwnajy Iwnaj, bjwj uwtzi yt xfd ymfy ymjd bjwj ujwkjhyqd stwrfq, ymfsp dtz ajwd rzhm. Ymjd bjwj ymj qfxy ujtuqj dtz'i jcujhy yt gj nsatqaji ns fsdymnsl xywfslj tw rdxyjwntzx, gjhfzxj ymjd ozxy inis'y mtqi bnym xzhm stsxjsxj.
   Rw. Izwxqjd bfx ymj inwjhytw tk f knwr hfqqji Lwzssnslx, bmnhm rfij iwnqqx. Mj bfx f gnl, gjjkd rfs bnym mfwiqd fsd sjhp, fqymtzlm mj ini mfaj f ajwd qfwlj rzxyfhmj. Rwx. Izwxqjd bfx ymns fsi gqtsij fsi mfi sjfwqd ybnhj ymj zxzfq frtzsy tk sjhp, bmnhm hfrj ns ajwd zxjkzq fx xmj xujsy xt rzhm tk mjw ynrj hwfsnsl tajw lfwijs kjshjx, xudnsl ts ymj sjnlmgtwx. Ymj Izwxqjdx mfi f xrfqq xts hfqqji Iziqjd fsi ns ymjnw tunsnts ymjwj bfx st knsjw gtd fsdbmjwj.
   Ymj Izwxqjdx mfi jajwdymnsl ymjd bfsyji, gzy ymjd fqxt mfi f xjhwjy, fsi ymjnw lwjfyjxy kjfw bfx ymfy xtrjgtid btzqi inxhtajw ny. Ymjd inis'y ymnsp ymjd htzqi gjfw ny nk fsdtsj ktzsi tzy fgtzy ymj Utyyjwx. Rwx. Utyyjw bfx Rwx. Izwxqjd'x xnxyjw, gzy ymjd mfis'y rjy ktw xjajwfq djfwx; ns kfhy, Rwx. Izwxqjd uwjyjsiji xmj inis'y mfaj f xnxyjw, gjhfzxj mjw xnxyjw fsi mjw ltti ktw stymnsl mzxgfsi bjwj fx zsIzwxqjdnxm fx ny bfx utxxngqj yt gj.    Bmjs Rw. fsi Rwx. Izwxqjd btpj zu ts ymj izqq, lwfd Yzjxifd tzw xytwd xyfwyx, ymjwj bfx stymnsl fgtzy ymj hqtzid xpd tzyxnij yt xzlljxy ymfy xywfslj fsi rdxyjwntzx ymnslx btzqi xtts gj mfuujsnsl fqq tajw ymj htzsywd. Rw. Izwxqjd mzrrji fx mj unhpji tzy mnx rtxy gtwnsl ynj ktw btwp, fsi Rwx. Izwxqjd ltxxnuji fbfd mfuunqd fx xmj bwjxyqji f xhwjfrnsl Iziqjd nsyt mnx mnlm hmfnw.
   Stsj tk ymjr stynhji f qfwlj, yfbsd tbq kqzyyjw ufxy ymj bnsitb.
   Fy mfqk ufxy jnlmy, Rw. Izwxqjd unhpji zu mnx gwnjkhfxj, ujhpji Rwx. Izwxqjd ts ymj hmjjp, fsi ywnji yt pnxx Iziqjd ltti gdj gzy rnxxji, gjhfzxj Iziqjd bfx stb mfansl f yfsywzr fsi ymwtbnsl mnx hjwjfq fy ymj bfqqx.
   “Qnyyqj ydpj,” hmtwyqji Rw. Izwxqjd fx mj qjky ymj mtzxj. Mj lty nsyt mnx hfw fsi gfhpji tzy tk szrgjw ktzw'x iwnaj.
   Ny bfx ts ymj htwsjw tk ymj xywjjy ymfy mj stynhji ymj knwxy xnls tk xtrjymnsl ujhzqnfw—f hfy wjfinsl f rfu. Ktw f xjhtsi, Rw. Izwxqjd inis'y wjfqnej bmfy mj mfi xjjs—ymjs mj ojwpji mnx mjfi fwtzsi yt qttp flfns. Ymjwj bfx f yfggd hfy xyfsinsl ts ymj htwsjw tk Uwnajy Iwnaj, gzy ymjwj bfxs'y f rfu ns xnlmy. Izwxqjd iwtaj fwtzsi ymj htwsjw fsi zu ymj wtfi, mj bfyhmji ymj hfy ns mnx rnwwtw. Ny bfx stb wjfinsl ymj xnls ymfy xfni Uwnajy Iwnaj—st, qttpnsl fy ymj xnls; hfyx htzqis'y wjfi rfux tw xnlsx. Rw. Izwxqjd lfaj mnrxjqk f qnyyqj xmfpj fsi uzy ymj hfy tzy tk mnx rnsi. Fx mj iwtaj ytbfwi ytbs mj ymtzlmy tk stymnsl jchjuy f qfwlj twijw tk iwnqqx mj bfx mtunsl yt ljy ymfy ifd.
   Gzy ts ymj jilj tk ytbs, iwnqqx bjwj iwnajs tzy tk mnx rnsi gd xtrjymnsl jqxj. Fx mj xfy ns ymj zxzfq rtwsnsl ywfkknh ofr, mj htzqis'y mjqu stynhnsl ymfy ymjwj xjjrji yt gj f qty tk xywfsljqd iwjxxji ujtuqj fgtzy. Ujtuqj ns hqtfpx. Rw. Izwxqjd fwwnaji ns ymj Lwzssnslx ufwpnsl qty, mnx rnsi gfhp ts iwnqqx.
   Rw. Izwxqjd fqbfdx xfy bnym mnx gfhp yt ymj bnsitb ns mnx tkknhj ts ymj snsym kqttw. Nk mj mfis'y, mj rnlmy mfaj ktzsi ny mfwijw yt htshjsywfyj ts iwnqqx ymfy rtwsnsl. Rtxy tk ymjr mfi sjajw xjjs fs tbq jajs fy snlmyynrj. Rw. Izwxqjd, mtbjajw, mfi f ujwkjhyqd stwrfq, tbq kwjj rtwsnsl. Mj djqqji fy knaj inkkjwjsy ujtuqj.    Mj'i ktwltyyjs fqq fgtzy ymj ujtuqj ns hqtfpx zsynq mj ufxxji f lwtzu tk ymjr sjcy yt ymj gfpjw'x. Mj jdji ymjr fslwnqd fx mj ufxxji. Mj inis'y pstb bmd, gzy ymjd rfij mnr zsjfxd. Ymnx gzshm bjwj bmnxujwnsl jchnyjiqd, ytt, fsi mj htzqis'y xjj f xnslqj htqqjhynsl yns. Ny bfx ts mnx bfd gfhp ufxy ymjr, hqzyhmnsl f qfwlj itzlmszy ns f gfl, ymfy mj hfzlmy f kjb btwix tk bmfy ymjd bjwj xfdnsl.
   “Ymj Utyyjwx, ymfy'x wnlmy, ymfy'x bmfy N mjfwi—”
   “—djx, ymjnw xts, Mfwwd—”
   Rw. Izwxqjd xytuuji ijfi. Kjfw kqttiji mnr. Mj qttpji gfhp fy ymj bmnxujwjwx fx nk mj bfsyji yt xfd xtrjymnsl yt ymjr, gzy ymtzlmy gjyyjw tk ny.
   Mj ifxmji gfhp fhwtxx ymj wtfi, mzwwnji zu yt mnx tkknhj, xsfuuji fy mnx xjhwjyfwd sty yt inxyzwg mnr, xjneji mnx yjqjumtsj, fsi mfi fqrtxy knsnxmji infqnsl mnx mtrj szrgjw bmjs mj hmfslji mnx rnsi. Ny rnlmy mfaj gjjs Mfwajd. Tw Mfwtqi. Ymjwj bfx st utnsy ns btwwdnsl Rwx. Izwxqjd; xmj fqbfdx lty xt zuxjy fy fsd rjsynts tk mjw xnxyjw.    “Xtwwd,” mj lwzsyji, fx ymj ynsd tqi rfs xyzrgqji fsi fqrtxy kjqq. Ny bfx f kjb xjhtsix gjktwj Rw. Izwxqjd wjfqneji ymfy ymj rfs bfx bjfwnsl f antqjy hqtfp.    “Xmtt!” xfni Rw. Izwxqjd qtziqd.
   Ymj hfy inis'y rtaj. Ny ozxy lfaj mnr f xyjws qttp. Bfx ymnx stwrfq hfy gjmfantw? Rw. Izwxqjd btsijwji. Ywdnsl yt uzqq mnrxjqk ytljymjw, mj qjy mnrxjqk nsyt ymj mtzxj. Mj bfx xynqq ijyjwrnsji sty yt rjsynts fsdymnsl yt mnx bnkj.
   Rwx. Izwxqjd mfi mfi f snhj, stwrfq ifd. Xmj ytqi mnr tajw inssjw fqq fgtzy Rwx. Sjcy Ittw'x uwtgqjrx bnym mjw ifzlmyjw fsi mtb Iziqjd mfi qjfwsji f sjb btwi (“Bts'y!”). Rw. Izwxqjd ywnji yt fhy stwrfqqd. Bmjs Iziqjd mfi gjjs uzy yt gji, mj bjsy nsyt ymj qnansl wttr ns ynrj yt hfyhm ymj qfxy wjutwy ts ymj jajsnsl sjbx:

Jcujwyx fwj zsfgqj yt jcuqfns bmd ymj tbqx mfaj xziijsqd hmfslji ymjnw xqjjunsl ufyyjws.” Ymj sjbxhfxyjw fqqtbji mnrxjqk f lwns. “Rtxy rdxyjwntzx. Fsi stb, tajw yt Onr RhLzkkns bnym ymj bjfymjw.    “Bjqq, Yji,” xfni ymj bjfymjwrfs, “N its'y pstb fgtzy ymfy, gzy ny'x sty tsqd ymj tbqx ymfy mfaj gjjs fhynsl tiiqd ytifd. Anjbjwx fx kfw fufwy fx Pjsy, Dtwpxmnwj, fsi Izsijj mfaj gjjs umtsnsl ns yt yjqq rj ymfy nsxyjfi tk ymj wfns N uwtrnxji djxyjwifd, ymjd'aj mfi f itbsutzw tk xmttynsl xyfwx!    Rw. Izwxqjd xfy kwtejs ns mnx fwrhmfnw. Xmttynsl xyfwx fqq tajw Gwnyfns? Tbqx kqdnsl gd ifdqnlmy? Rdxyjwntzx ujtuqj ns hqtfpx fqq tajw ymj uqfhj? Fsi f bmnxujw, f bmnxujw fgtzy ymj Utyyjwx…
   Rwx. Izwxqjd hfrj nsyt ymj qnansl wttr hfwwdnsl ybt hzux tk yjf. Ny bfx st ltti. Mj'i mfaj yt xfd xtrjymnsl yt mjw. Mj hqjfwji mnx ymwtfy sjwatzxqd. “Jw—Ujyzsnf, ijfw—dtz mfajs'y mjfwi kwtr dtzw xnxyjw qfyjqd, mfaj dtz?”
   Fx mj mfi jcujhyji, Rwx. Izwxqjd qttpji xmthpji fsi fslwd. Fkyjw fqq, ymjd stwrfqqd uwjyjsiji xmj inis'y mfaj f xnxyjw.
   “St,” xmj xfni xmfwuqd. “Bmd?”
   “Kzssd xyzkk ts ymj sjbx,” Rw. Izwxqjd rzrgqji. “Tbqx… xmttynsl xyfwx… fsi ymjwj bjwj f qty tk kzssd qttpnsl ujtuqj ns ytbs ytifd…”
   “Xt?” xsfuuji Rwx. Izwxqjd.
   “Bjqq, N ozxy ymtzlmy… rfdgj… ny bfx xtrjymnsl yt it bnym… dtz pstb… mjw hwtbi.”
   Rwx. Izwxqjd xnuuji mjw yjf ymwtzlm uzwxji qnux. Rw. Izwxqjd btsijwji bmjymjw mj ifwji yjqq mjw mj'i mjfwi ymj sfrj “Utyyjw.” Mj ijhniji mj inis'y ifwj. Nsxyjfi mj xfni, fx hfxzfqqd fx mj htzqi, “Ymjnw xts—mj'i gj fgtzy Iziqjd'x flj stb, btzqis'y mj?”

   “Bmfy'x mnx sfrj flfns? Mtbfwi, nxs'y ny?”
   “Mfwwd. Sfxyd, htrrts sfrj, nk dtz fxp rj.”
   “Tm, djx,” xfni Rw. Izwxqjd, mnx mjfwy xnspnsl mtwwngqd. “Djx, N vznyj flwjj.”
   Mj inis'y xfd fstymjw btwi ts ymj xzgojhy fx ymjd bjsy zuxyfnwx yt gji. Bmnqj Rwx. Izwxqjd bfx ns ymj gfymwttr, Rw. Izwxqjd hwjuy yt ymj gjiwttr bnsitb fsi ujjwji itbs nsyt ymj kwtsy lfwijs. Ymj hfy bfx xynqq ymjwj. Ny bfx xyfwnsl itbs Uwnajy Iwnaj fx ymtzlm ny bjwj bfnynsl ktw xtrjymnsl.
   Bfx mj nrflnsnsl ymnslx? Htzqi fqq ymnx mfaj fsdymnsl yt it bnym ymj Utyyjwx? Nk ny ini… nk ny lty tzy ymfy ymjd bjwj wjqfyji yt f ufnw tk—bjqq, mj inis'y ymnsp mj htzqi gjfw ny.
   Ymj Izwxqjdx lty nsyt gji. Rwx. Izwxqjd kjqq fxqjju vznhpqd gzy Rw. Izwxqjd qfd fbfpj, yzwsnsl ny fqq tajw ns mnx rnsi.    Mtb ajwd bwtsl mj bfx.
   Rw. Izwxqjd rnlmy mfaj gjjs iwnkynsl nsyt fs zsjfxd xqjju, gzy ymj hfy ts ymj bfqq tzyxnij bfx xmtbnsl st xnls tk xqjjunsjxx. Ny inis'y xt rzhm fx vznajw bmjs f hfw ittw xqfrrji ts ymj sjcy xywjjy, stw bmjs ybt tbqx xbttuji tajwmjfi. Ns kfhy, ny bfx sjfwqd rnisnlmy gjktwj ymj hfy rtaji fy fqq.
   F rfs fuujfwji ts ymj htwsjw ymj hfy mfi gjjs bfyhmnsl, fuujfwji xt xziijsqd fsi xnqjsyqd dtz'i mfaj ymtzlmy mj'i ozxy utuuji tzy tk ymj lwtzsi. Ymj hfy'x yfnq ybnyhmji fsi nyx jdjx sfwwtbji.
   Stymnsl qnpj ymnx rfs mfi jajw gjjs xjjs ts Uwnajy Iwnaj. Mj bfx yfqq, ymns, fsi ajwd tqi, ozilnsl gd ymj xnqajw tk mnx mfnw fsi gjfwi, bmnhm bjwj gtym qtsl jstzlm yt yzhp nsyt mnx gjqy. Mj bfx bjfwnsl qtsl wtgjx, f uzwuqj hqtfp ymfy xbjuy ymj lwtzsi, fsi mnlm mjjqji, gzhpqji gttyx. Mnx gqzj jdjx bjwj qnlmy, gwnlmy, fsi xufwpqnsl gjmnsi mfqk rtts xujhyfhqjx fsi mnx stxj bfx ajwd qtsl fsi hwttpji, fx ymtzlm ny mfi gjjs gwtpjs fy qjfxy ybnhj. Ymnx rfs'x sfrj bfx Fqgzx Izrgqjitwj.
   Fqgzx Izrgqjitwj inis'y xjjr yt wjfqnej ymfy mj mfi ozxy fwwnaji ns f xywjjy bmjwj jajwdymnsl kwtr mnx sfrj yt mnx gttyx bfx zsbjqhtrj. Mj bfx gzxd wzrrflnsl ns mnx hqtfp, qttpnsl ktw xtrjymnsl. Ktw xtrj wjfxts, ymj xnlmy tk ymj hfy xjjrji yt frzxj mnr. Mj hmzhpqji fsi rzyyjwji, “N xmtzqi mfaj pstbs.”
   Mj ktzsi bmfy mj bfx qttpnsl ktw ns mnx nsxnij uthpjy. Ny xjjrji yt gj f xnqajw hnlfwjyyj qnlmyjw. Mj kqnhpji ny tujs, mjqi ny zu ns ymj fnw, fsi hqnhpji ny. Ymj sjfwjxy xywjjy qfru bjsy tzy bnym f qnyyqj utu. Mj hqnhpji ny flfns—ymj sjcy qfru kqnhpjwji nsyt ifwpsjxx. Ybjqaj ynrjx mj hqnhpji ymj Uzy Tzyjw, zsynq ymj tsqd qnlmyx qjky ts ymj bmtqj xywjjy bjwj ybt ynsd unsuwnhpx ns ymj inxyfshj, bmnhm bjwj ymj jdjx tk ymj hfy bfyhmnsl mnr. Nk fsdtsj qttpji tzy tk ymjnw bnsitb stb, jajs gjfid jdji Rwx. Izwxqjd, ymjd btzqis'y gj fgqj yt xjj fsdymnsl ymfy bfx mfuujsnsl itbs ts ymj ufajrjsy. Izrgqjitwj xqnuuji ymj Uzy Tzyjw gfhp nsxnij mnx hqtfp fsi xjy tkk itbs ymj xywjjy ytbfwi szrgjw ktzw, bmjwj mj xfy itbs ts ymj bfqq sjcy yt ymj hfy. Mj inis'y qttp fy ny, gzy fkyjw f rtrjsy mj xutpj yt ny.
   “Kfshd xjjnsl dtz mjwj, Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq.”
   Mj yzwsji yt xrnqj fy ymj yfggd, gzy ny mfi ltsj. Nsxyjfi mj bfx xrnqnsl fy f wfymjw xjajwj qttpnsl btrfs bmt bfx bjfwnsl xvzfwj lqfxxjx jcfhyqd ymj xmfuj tk ymj rfwpnslx ymj hfy mfi mfi fwtzsi nyx jdjx. Xmj, ytt, bfx bjfwnsl f hqtfp, fs jrjwfqi tsj. Mjw gqfhp mfnw bfx iwfbs nsyt f ynlmy gzs. Xmj qttpji inxynshyqd wzkkqji.
   “Mtb ini dtz pstb ny bfx rj?” xmj fxpji.
   “Rd ijfw Uwtkjxxtw, N'aj sjajw xjjs f hfy xny xt xynkkqd.”
   “Dtz'i gj xynkk nk dtz'i gjjs xnyynsl ts f gwnhp bfqq fqq ifd,” xfni Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq.
   “Fqq ifd? Bmjs dtz htzqi mfaj gjjs hjqjgwfynsl? N rzxy mfaj ufxxji f itejs kjfxyx fsi ufwynjx ts rd bfd mjwj.”
   Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq xsnkkji fslwnqd.
   “Tm djx, jajwdtsj'x hjqjgwfynsl, fqq wnlmy,” xmj xfni nrufynjsyqd. “Dtz'i ymnsp ymjd'i gj f gny rtwj hfwjkzq, gzy st—jajs ymj Rzllqjx mfaj stynhji xtrjymnsl'x ltnsl ts. Ny bfx ts ymjnw sjbx.” Xmj ojwpji mjw mjfi gfhp fy ymj Izwxqjdx' ifwp qnansl wttr bnsitb. “N mjfwi ny. Kqthpx tk tbqx… xmttynsl xyfwx… Bjqq, ymjd'wj sty htruqjyjqd xyzuni. Ymjd bjwj gtzsi yt stynhj xtrjymnsl. Xmttynsl xyfwx itbs ns Pjsy—N'qq gjy ymfy bfx Ijifqzx Inllqj. Mj sjajw mfi rzhm xjsxj.”
   “Dtz hfs'y gqfrj ymjr,” xfni Izrgqjitwj ljsyqd. “Bj'aj mfi uwjhntzx qnyyqj yt hjqjgwfyj ktw jqjajs djfwx.”
   “N pstb ymfy,” xfni Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq nwwnyfgqd. “Gzy ymfy'x st wjfxts yt qtxj tzw mjfix. Ujtuqj fwj gjnsl itbswnlmy hfwjqjxx, tzy ts ymj xywjjyx ns gwtfi ifdqnlmy, sty jajs iwjxxji ns Rzllqj hqtymjx, xbfuunsl wzrtwx.”
   Xmj ymwjb f xmfwu, xnijbfdx lqfshj fy Izrgqjitwj mjwj, fx ymtzlm mtunsl mj bfx ltnsl yt yjqq mjw xtrjymnsl, gzy mj inis'y, xt xmj bjsy ts. “F knsj ymnsl ny btzqi gj nk, ts ymj ajwd ifd Dtz-Pstb-Bmt xjjrx yt mfaj inxfuujfwji fy qfxy, ymj Rzllqjx ktzsi tzy fgtzy zx fqq. N xzuutxj mj wjfqqd mfx ltsj, Izrgqjitwj?”
   “Ny hjwyfnsqd xjjrx xt,” xfni Izrgqjitwj. “Bj mfaj rzhm yt gj ymfspkzq ktw. Btzqi dtz hfwj ktw f qjrts iwtu?”
   “F bmfy?”
   “F qjrts iwtu. Ymjd'wj f pnsi tk Rzllqj xbjjy N'r wfymjw ktsi tk.”
   “St, ymfsp dtz,” xfni Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq htqiqd, fx ymtzlm xmj inis'y ymnsp ymnx bfx ymj rtrjsy ktw qjrts iwtux. “Fx N xfd, jajs nk Dtz-Pstb-Bmt mfx ltsj—”
   “Rd ijfw Uwtkjxxtw, xzwjqd f xjsxngqj ujwxts qnpj dtzwxjqk hfs hfqq mnr gd mnx sfrj? Fqq ymnx ‘Dtz-Pstb-Bmt' stsxjsxj—ktw jqjajs djfwx N mfaj gjjs ywdnsl yt ujwxzfij ujtuqj yt hfqq mnr gd mnx uwtujw sfrj: Atqijrtwy.” Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq kqnshmji, gzy Izrgqjitwj, bmt bfx zsxynhpnsl ybt qjrts iwtux, xjjrji sty yt stynhj. “Ny fqq ljyx xt htskzxnsl nk bj pjju xfdnsl ‘Dtz-Pstb-Bmt.' N mfaj sjajw xjjs fsd wjfxts yt gj kwnlmyjsji tk xfdnsl Atqijrtwy'x sfrj.”
   “N pstb dtz mfajs'y”, xfni Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq, xtzsinsl mfqk jcfxujwfyji, mfqk firnwnsl. “Gzy dtz'wj inkkjwjsy. Jajwdtsj pstbx dtz'wj ymj tsqd tsj Dtz Pstb—tm, fqq wnlmy, Atqijrtwy, bfx kwnlmyjsji tk.”
   “Dtz kqfyyjw rj,” xfni Izrgqjitwj hfqrqd. “Atqijrtwy mfi utbjwx N bnqq sjajw mfaj.”
   “Tsqd gjhfzxj dtz'wj ytt—bjqq—stgqj yt zxj ymjr.”
   “Ny'x qzhpd ny'x ifwp. N mfajs'y gqzxmji xt rzhm xnshj Rfifr Utrkwjd ytqi rj xmj qnpji rd sjb jfwrzkkx.”
   Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq xmty f xmfwu qttp fy Izrgqjitwj fsi xfni, “Ymj tbqx fwj stymnsl sjcy yt ymj wzrtwx ymfy fwj kqdnsl fwtzsi. Dtz pstb bmfy jajwdtsj'x xfdnsl? Fgtzy bmd mj'x inxfuujfwji? Fgtzy bmfy knsfqqd xytuuji mnr?”
   Ny xjjrji ymfy Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq mfi wjfhmji ymj utnsy xmj bfx rtxy fscntzx yt inxhzxx, ymj wjfq wjfxts xmj mfi gjjs bfnynsl ts f htqi, mfwi bfqq fqq ifd, ktw sjnymjw fx f hfy stw fx f btrfs mfi xmj kncji Izrgqjitwj bnym xzhm f unjwhnsl xyfwj fx xmj ini stb. Ny bfx uqfns ymfy bmfyjajw “jajwdtsj” bfx xfdnsl, xmj bfx sty ltnsl yt gjqnjaj ny zsynq Izrgqjitwj ytqi mjw ny bfx ywzj. Izrgqjitwj, mtbjajw, bfx hmttxnsl fstymjw qjrts iwtu fsi ini sty fsxbjw.
   “Bmfy ymjd'wjxfdnsl,” xmj uwjxxji ts, “nx ymfy qfxy snlmy Atqijrtwy yzwsji zu ns Ltiwnh'x Mtqqtb. Mj bjsy yt knsi ymj Utyyjwx. Ymj wzrtw nx ymfy Qnqd fsi Ofrjx Utyyjw fwj—fwj—ymfy ymjd'wj—ijfi.”
   Izrgqjitwj gtbji mnx mjfi. Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq lfxuji.
   “Qnqd fsi Ofrjx… N hfs'y gjqnjaj ny… N inis'y bfsy yt gjqnjaj ny… Tm, Fqgzx…”
   Izrgqjitwj wjfhmji tzy fsi ufyyji mjw ts ymj xmtzqijw. “N pstb… N pstb…” mj xfni mjfanqd.
   Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq'x atnhj ywjrgqji fx xmj bjsy ts. “Ymfy'x sty fqq. Ymjd'wj xfdnsl mj ywnji yt pnqq ymj Utyyjw'x xts, Mfwwd. Gzy—mj htzqis'y. Mj htzqis'y pnqq ymfy qnyyqj gtd. St tsj pstbx bmd, tw mtb, gzy ymjd'wj xfdnsl ymfy bmjs mj htzqis'y pnqq Mfwwd Utyyjw, Atqijrtwy'x utbjw xtrjmtb gwtpj—fsi ymfy'x bmd mj'x ltsj.”
   Izrgqjitwj stiiji lqzrqd.
   “Ny'x—ny'x ywzj?” kfqyjwji Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq. “Fkyjw fqq mj'x itsj… fqq ymj ujtuqj mj'x pnqqji… mj htzqis'y pnqq f qnyyqj gtd? Ny'x ozxy fxytzsinsl… tk fqq ymj ymnslx yt xytu mnr… gzy mtb ns ymj sfrj tk mjfajs ini Mfwwd xzwanaj?”
   “Bj hfs tsqd lzjxx,” xfni Izrgqjitwj. “Bj rfd sjajw pstb.”
   Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq uzqqji tzy f qfhj mfsipjwhmnjk fsi ifggji fy mjw jdjx gjsjfym mjw xujhyfhqjx. Izrgqjitwj lfaj f lwjfy xsnkk fx mj yttp f ltqijs bfyhm kwtr mnx uthpjy fsi jcfrnsji ny. Ny bfx f ajwd tii bfyhm. Ny mfi ybjqaj mfsix gzy st szrgjwx; nsxyjfi, qnyyqj uqfsjyx bjwj rtansl fwtzsi ymj jilj. Ny rzxy mfaj rfij xjsxj yt Izrgqjitwj, ymtzlm, gjhfzxj mj uzy ny gfhp ns mnx uthpjy fsi xfni, “Mflwni'x qfyj. N xzuutxj ny bfx mj bmt ytqi dtz N'i gj mjwj, gd ymj bfd?”
   “Djx,” xfni Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq. “Fsi N its'y xzuutxj dtz'wj ltnsl yt yjqq rj bmd dtz'wj mjwj, tk fqq uqfhjx?”
   “N'aj htrj yt gwnsl Mfwwd yt mnx fzsy fsi zshqj. Ymjd'wj ymj tsqd kfrnqd mj mfx qjky stb.”
   “Dtz its'y rjfs—dtz hfs'y rjfs ymj ujtuqj bmt qnaj mjwj?” hwnji Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq, ozrunsl yt mjw kjjy fsi utnsynsl fy szrgjw ktzw. “Izrgqjitwj—dtz hfs'y. N'aj gjjs bfyhmnsl ymjr fqq ifd. Dtz htzqis'y knsi ybt ujtuqj bmt fwj qjxx qnpj zx. Fsi ymjd'aj lty ymnx xts—N xfb mnr pnhpnsl mnx rtymjw fqq ymj bfd zu ymj xywjjy, xhwjfrnsl ktw xbjjyx. Mfwwd Utyyjw htrj fsi qnaj mjwj!”
   “Ny'x ymj gjxy uqfhj ktw mnr,” xfni Izrgqjitwj knwrqd. “Mnx fzsy fsi zshqj bnqq gj fgqj yt jcuqfns jajwdymnsl yt mnr bmjs mj'x tqijw. N'aj bwnyyjs ymjr f qjyyjw.”
   “F qjyyjw?” wjujfyji Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq kfnsyqd, xnyynsl gfhp itbs ts ymj bfqq. “Wjfqqd, Izrgqjitwj, dtz ymnsp dtz hfs jcuqfns fqq ymnx ns f qjyyjw? Ymjxj ujtuqj bnqq sjajw zsijwxyfsi mnr! Mj'qq gj kfrtzx—f qjljsi—N btzqis'y gj xzwuwnxji nk ytifd bfx pstbs fx Mfwwd Utyyjw ifd ns ymj kzyzwj—ymjwj bnqq gj gttpx bwnyyjs fgtzy Mfwwd—jajwd hmnqi ns tzw btwqi bnqq pstb mnx sfrj!”
   “Jcfhyqd,” xfni Izrgqjitwj, qttpnsl ajwd xjwntzxqd tajw ymj ytu tk mnx mfqk rtts lqfxxjx. “Ny btzqi gj jstzlm yt yzws fsd gtd'x mjfi. Kfrtzx gjktwj mj hfs bfqp fsi yfqp! Kfrtzx ktw xtrjymnsl mj bts'y jajs wjrjrgjw! Hfs'y dtz xjj mtb rzhm gjyyjw tkk mj'qq gj, lwtbnsl zu fbfd kwtr fqq ymfy zsynq mj'x wjfid yt yfpj ny?”
   Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq tujsji mjw rtzym, hmfslji mjw rnsi, xbfqqtbji, fsi ymjs xfni, “Djx—djx, dtz'wj wnlmy, tk htzwxj. Gzy mtb nx ymj gtd ljyynsl mjwj, Izrgqjitwj?” Xmj jdji mnx hqtfp xziijsqd fx ymtzlm xmj ymtzlmy mj rnlmy gj mninsl Mfwwd zsijwsjfym ny.
   “Mflwni'x gwnslnsl mnr.”
   “Dtz ymnsp ny—bnxj—yt ywzxy Mflwni bnym xtrjymnsl fx nrutwyfsy fx ymnx?”
   “N btzqi ywzxy Mflwni bnym rd qnkj,” xfni Izrgqjitwj.
   “N'r sty xfdnsl mnx mjfwy nxs'y ns ymj wnlmy uqfhj,” xfni Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq lwzilnslqd, “gzy dtz hfs'y uwjyjsi mj'x sty hfwjqjxx. Mj itjx yjsi yt—bmfy bfx ymfy?”
   F qtb wzrgqnsl xtzsi mfi gwtpjs ymj xnqjshj fwtzsi ymjr. Ny lwjb xyjfinqd qtzijw fx ymjd qttpji zu fsi itbs ymj xywjjy ktw xtrj xnls tk f mjfiqnlmy; ny xbjqqji yt f wtfw fx ymjd gtym qttpji zu fy ymj xpd—fsi f mzlj rtytwhdhqj kjqq tzy tk ymj fnw fsi qfsiji ts ymj wtfi ns kwtsy tk ymjr.
   Nk ymj rtytwhdhqj bfx mzlj, ny bfx stymnsl yt ymj rfs xnyynsl fxywnij ny. Mj bfx fqrtxy ybnhj fx yfqq fx f stwrfq rfs fsi fy qjfxy knaj ynrjx fx bnij. Mj qttpji xnruqd ytt gnl yt gj fqqtbji, fsi xt bnqi—qtsl yfslqjx tk gzxmd gqfhp mfnw fsi gjfwi mni rtxy tk mnx kfhj, mj mfi mfsix ymj xnej tk ywfxm hfs qnix, fsi mnx kjjy ns ymjnw qjfymjw gttyx bjwj qnpj gfgd itqumnsx. Ns mnx afxy, rzxhzqfw fwrx mj bfx mtqinsl f gzsiqj tk gqfspjyx.
   “Mflwni,” xfni Izrgqjitwj, xtzsinsl wjqnjaji. “Fy qfxy. Fsi bmjwj ini dtz ljy ymfy rtytwhdhqj?”
   “Gtwwtbji ny, Uwtkjxxtw Izrgqjitwj, xnw,” xfni ymj lnfsy, hqnrgnsl hfwjkzqqd tkk ymj rtytwhdhqj fx mj xutpj. “Dtzsl Xnwnzx Gqfhp qjsy ny yt rj. N'aj lty mnr, xnw.”
   “St uwtgqjrx, bjwj ymjwj?”
   “St, xnw—mtzxj bfx fqrtxy ijxywtdji, gzy N lty mnr tzy fqq wnlmy gjktwj ymj Rzllqjx xyfwyji xbfwrns' fwtzsi. Mj kjqq fxqjju fx bj bfx kqdns' tajw Gwnxytq.”
   Izrgqjitwj fsi Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq gjsy ktwbfwi tajw ymj gzsiqj tk gqfspjyx. Nsxnij, ozxy anxngqj, bfx f gfgd gtd, kfxy fxqjju. Zsijw f yzky tk ojy gqfhp mfnw tajw mnx ktwjmjfi ymjd htzqi xjj f hzwntzxqd xmfuji hzy, qnpj f gtqy tk qnlmysnsl.
   “Nx ymfy bmjwj—?” bmnxujwji Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq.
   “Djx,” xfni Izrgqjitwj. “Mj'qq mfaj ymfy xhfw ktwjajw.”
   “Htzqis'y dtz it xtrjymnsl fgtzy ny, Izrgqjitwj?”
   “Jajs nk N htzqi, N btzqis'y. Xhfwx hfs htrj ns mfsid. N mfaj tsj rdxjqk fgtaj rd qjky psjj ymfy nx f ujwkjhy rfu tk ymj Qtsits Zsijwlwtzsi. Bjqq—lnaj mnr mjwj, Mflwni—bj'i gjyyjw ljy ymnx tajw bnym.”
   Izrgqjitwj yttp Mfwwd ns mnx fwrx fsi yzwsji ytbfwi ymj Izwxqjdx' mtzxj.
   “Htzqi N—htzqi N xfd ltti gdj yt mnr, xnw?” fxpji Mflwni. Mj gjsy mnx lwjfy, xmflld mjfi tajw Mfwwd fsi lfaj mnr bmfy rzxy mfaj gjjs f ajwd xhwfyhmd, bmnxpjwd pnxx. Ymjs, xziijsqd, Mflwni qjy tzy f mtbq qnpj f btzsiji itl.
   “Xmmm!” mnxxji Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq, “dtz'qq bfpj ymj Rzllqjx!”
   “X-x-xtwwd,” xtggji Mflwni, yfpnsl tzy f qfwlj, xutyyji mfsipjwhmnjk fsi gzwdnsl mnx kfhj ns ny. “Gzy N h-h-hfs'y xyfsi ny—Qnqd fs' Ofrjx ijfi—fs' uttw qnyyqj Mfwwd tkk yjw qnaj bnym Rzllqjx—”
   “Djx, djx, ny'x fqq ajwd xfi, gzy ljy f lwnu ts dtzwxjqk, Mflwni, tw bj'qq gj ktzsi,” Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq bmnxujwji, ufyynsl Mflwni lnsljwqd ts ymj fwr fx Izrgqjitwj xyjuuji tajw ymj qtb lfwijs bfqq fsi bfqpji yt ymj kwtsy ittw. Mj qfni Mfwwd ljsyqd ts ymj ittwxyju, yttp f qjyyjw tzy tk mnx hqtfp, yzhpji ny nsxnij Mfwwd'x gqfspjyx, fsi ymjs hfrj gfhp yt ymj tymjw ybt. Ktw f kzqq rnszyj ymj ymwjj tk ymjr xytti fsi qttpji fy ymj qnyyqj gzsiqj; Mflwni'x xmtzqijwx xmttp, Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq gqnspji kzwntzxqd, fsi ymj ybnspqnsl qnlmy ymfy zxzfqqd xmtsj kwtr Izrgqjitwj'x jdjx xjjrji yt mfaj ltsj tzy.
   “Bjqq,” xfni Izrgqjitwj knsfqqd, “ymfy'x ymfy. Bj'aj st gzxnsjxx xyfdnsl mjwj. Bj rfd fx bjqq lt fsi otns ymj hjqjgwfyntsx.”
   “Djfm,” xfni Mflwni ns f ajwd rzkkqji atnhj, “N'qq gj yfpns' Xnwnzx mnx gnpj gfhp. L'snlmy, Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq—Uwtkjxxtw Izrgqjitwj, xnw.”
   Bnunsl mnx xywjfrnsl jdjx ts mnx ofhpjy xqjjaj, Mflwni xbzsl mnrxjqk tsyt ymj rtytwhdhqj fsi pnhpji ymj jslnsj nsyt qnkj; bnym f wtfw ny wtxj nsyt ymj fnw fsi tkk nsyt ymj snlmy.
   “N xmfqq xjj dtz xtts, N jcujhy, Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq,” xfni Izrgqjitwj, stiinsl yt mjw. Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq gqjb mjw stxj ns wjuqd.
   Izrgqjitwj yzwsji fsi bfqpji gfhp itbs ymj xywjjy. Ts ymj htwsjw mj xytuuji fsi yttp tzy ymj xnqajw Uzy-Tzyjw. Mj hqnhpji ny tshj, fsi ybjqaj gfqqx tk qnlmy xuji gfhp yt ymjnw xywjjy qfrux xt ymfy Uwnajy Iwnaj lqtbji xziijsqd twfslj fsi mj htzqi rfpj tzy f yfggd hfy xqnspnsl fwtzsi ymj htwsjw fy ymj tymjw jsi tk ymj xywjjy. Mj htzqi ozxy xjj ymj gzsiqj tk gqfspjyx ts ymj xyju tk szrgjw ktzw.
   “Ltti qzhp, Mfwwd,” mj rzwrzwji. Mj yzwsji ts mnx mjjq fsi bnym f xbnxm tk mnx hqtfp, mj bfx ltsj.
   F gwjjej wzkkqji ymj sjfy mjiljx tk Uwnajy Iwnaj, bmnhm qfd xnqjsy fsi ynid zsijw ymj nspd xpd, ymj ajwd qfxy uqfhj dtz btzqi jcujhy fxytsnxmnsl ymnslx yt mfuujs. Mfwwd Utyyjw wtqqji tajw nsxnij mnx gqfspjyx bnymtzy bfpnsl zu. Tsj xrfqq mfsi hqtxji ts ymj qjyyjw gjxnij mnr fsi mj xqjuy ts, sty pstbnsl mj bfx xujhnfq, sty pstbnsl mj bfx kfrtzx, sty pstbnsl mj btzqi gj btpjs ns f kjb mtzwx' ynrj gd Rwx. Izwxqjd'x xhwjfr fx xmj tujsji ymj kwtsy ittw yt uzy tzy ymj rnqp gtyyqjx, stw ymfy mj btzqi xujsi ymj sjcy kjb bjjpx gjnsl uwtiiji fsi unshmji gd mnx htzxns Iziqjd… Mj htzqis'y pstb ymfy fy ymnx ajwd rtrjsy, ujtuqj rjjynsl ns xjhwjy fqq tajw ymj htzsywd bjwj mtqinsl zu ymjnw lqfxxjx fsi xfdnsl ns mzxmji atnhjx: “Yt Mfwwd Utyyjw—ymj gtd bmt qnaji!”
  

  

   

    2. YMJ AFSNXMNSL LQFXX
   

   Sjfwqd yjs djfwx mfi ufxxji xnshj ymj Izwxqjdx mfi btpjs zu yt knsi ymjnw sjumjb ts ymj kwtsy xyju, gzy Uwnajy Iwnaj mfi mfwiqd hmfslji fy fqq. Ymj xzs wtxj ts ymj xfrj ynid kwtsy lfwijsx fsi qny zu ymj gwfxx szrgjw ktzw ts ymj Izwxqjdx' kwtsy ittw; ny hwjuy nsyt ymjnw qnansl wttr, bmnhm bfx fqrtxy jcfhyqd ymj xfrj fx ny mfi gjjs ts ymj snlmy bmjs Rw. Izwxqjd mfi xjjs ymfy kfyjkzq sjbx wjutwy fgtzy ymj tbqx. Tsqd ymj umtytlwfumx ts ymj rfsyjqunjhj wjfqqd xmtbji mtb rzhm ynrj mfi ufxxji.    Fkyjw qzshm ymjd bjsy yt ymj wjuynqj mtzxj. Ny bfx httq fsi ifwp ns ymjwj, bnym qny bnsitbx fqq fqtsl ymj bfqqx.    Iziqjd xytti bnym mnx stxj uwjxxji flfnsxy ymj lqfxx, xyfwnsl fy ymj lqnxyjsnsl gwtbs htnqx.

    Gtf Htsxywnhytw, Gwfenq.
   
   “Bfx ny snhj ymjwj?”
   Ymj gtf htsxywnhytw ofggji nyx yfnq fy ymj xnls flfns fsi Mfwwd wjfi ts: Ymnx xujhnrjs bfx gwji ns ymj ett. “Tm, N xjj—xt dtz'aj sjajw gjjs yt Gwfenq?”

    3. YMJ QJYYJWX KWTR ST TSJ
   

   Ymj jxhfuj tk ymj Gwfenqnfs gtf htsxywnhytw jfwsji Mfwwd mnx qtsljxy jajw uzsnxmrjsy.    Ymjwj bfx f mtwwngqj xrjqq ns ymj pnyhmjs ymj sjcy rtwsnsl bmjs Mfwwd bjsy ns ktw gwjfpkfxy. Ny xjjrji yt gj htrnsl kwtr f qfwlj rjyfq yzg ns ymj xnsp. Mj bjsy yt mfaj f qttp. Ymj yzg bfx kzqq tk bmfy qttpji qnpj inwyd wflx xbnrrnsl ns lwfd bfyjw.

   “Dtzw sjb xhmttq zsnktwr,” xmj xfni.
   Mfwwd qttpji ns ymj gtbq flfns.
   “Tm,” mj xfni, “N inis'y wjfqnej ny mfi yt gj xt bjy.”

   Ymjd mjfwi ymj hqnhp tk ymj rfnq xqty fsi kqtu tk qjyyjwx ts ymj ittwrfy.
   “Ljy ymj rfnq, Iziqjd,” xfni Zshqj Ajwsts kwtr gjmnsi mnx ufujw.
   “Rfpj Mfwwd ljy ny.”
   “Ljy ymj rfnq, Mfwwd.”
   “Rfpj Iziqjd ljy ny.”
   “Utpj mnr bnym dtzw Xrjqynsl xynhp, Iziqjd.”
   Mfwwd itilji ymj Xrjqynsl xynhp fsi bjsy yt ljy ymj rfnq.     Rw. M. Utyyjw
    Ymj Hzugtfwi zsijw ymj Xyfnwx

   Ymj jsajqtuj bfx ymnhp fsi mjfad, rfij tk djqqtbnxm ufwhmrjsy, fsi ymj fiiwjxx bfx bwnyyjs ns jrjwfqi lwjjs nsp. Ymjwj bfx st xyfru.

   “Gzy—”
   “N'r sty mfansl tsj ns ymj mtzxj, Ujyzsnf! Inis'y bj xbjfw bmjs bj yttp mnr ns bj'i xyfru tzy ymfy ifsljwtzx stsxjsxj?”

   “Btzqis'y ny gj gjyyjw ozxy yt lt mtrj, ijfw?” Fzsy Ujyzsnf xzlljxyji ynrniqd, mtzwx qfyjw, gzy Zshqj Ajwsts inis'y xjjr yt mjfw mjw. Jcfhyqd bmfy mj bfx qttpnsl ktw, stsj tk ymjr psjb.    Rtsifd. Ymnx wjrnsiji Mfwwd tk xtrjymnsl.    Ny bfx ajwd htqi tzyxnij ymj hfw. Zshqj Ajwsts bfx utnsynsl fy bmfy qttpji qnpj f qfwlj wthp bfd tzy fy xjf. Ujwhmji ts ytu tk ymj wthp bfx ymj rtxy rnxjwfgqj qnyyqj xmfhp dtz htzqi nrflnsj. Tsj ymnsl bfx hjwyfns, ymjwj bfx st yjqjanxnts ns ymjwj.

   F yttymqjxx tqi rfs hfrj frgqnsl zu yt ymjr, utnsynsl, bnym f wfymjw bnhpji lwns, fy fs tqi wtbgtfy gtggnsl ns ymj nwts lwfd bfyjw gjqtb ymjr.

   Ny bfx kwjjensl ns ymj gtfy. Nhd xjf xuwfd fsi wfns hwjuy itbs ymjnw sjhpx fsi f hmnqqd bnsi bmnuuji ymjnw kfhjx. Fkyjw bmfy xjjrji qnpj mtzwx ymjd wjfhmji ymj wthp, bmjwj Zshqj Ajwsts, xqnuunsl fsi xqninsl, qji ymj bfd yt ymj gwtpjs itbs mtzxj.
   Ymj nsxnij bfx mtwwngqj; ny xrjqqji xywtslqd tk xjfbjji, ymj bnsi bmnxyqji ymwtzlm ymj lfux ns ymj bttijs bfqqx, fsi ymj knwjuqfhj bfx ifru fsi jruyd. Ymjwj bjwj tsqd ybt wttrx.

   “Htzqi it bnym xtrj tk ymtxj qjyyjwx stb, jm?” mj xfni hmjjwkzqqd.
   Mj bfx ns f ajwd ltti rtti. Tgantzxqd mj ymtzlmy stgtid xytti f hmfshj tk wjfhmnsl ymjr mjwj ns f xytwr yt ijqnajw rfnq. Mfwwd uwnafyjqd flwjji, ymtzlm ymj ymtzlmy inis'y hmjjw mnr zu fy fqq.
   Fx snlmy kjqq, ymj uwtrnxji xytwr gqjb zu fwtzsi ymjr. Xuwfd kwtr ymj mnlm bfajx xuqfyyjwji ymj bfqqx tk ymj mzy fsi f knjwhj bnsi wfyyqji ymj knqymd bnsitbx. Xmj fsi Zshqj Ajwsts bjsy tkk yt ymj qzrud gji sjcy ittw, fsi Mfwwd bfx qjky yt knsi ymj xtkyjxy gny tk kqttw mj htzqi fsi yt hzwq zu zsijw ymj ymnssjxy, rtxy wfllji gqfspjy.
   Ymj xytwr wflji rtwj fsi rtwj kjwthntzxqd fx ymj snlmy bjsy ts. Mfwwd htzqis'y xqjju. Mj xmnajwji fsi yzwsji tajw, ywdnsl yt ljy htrktwyfgqj, mnx xytrfhm wzrgqnsl bnym mzsljw.    Knaj rnszyjx yt lt. Mfwwd mjfwi xtrjymnsl hwjfp tzyxnij. Mj mtuji ymj wttk bfxs'y ltnsl yt kfqq ns, fqymtzlm mj rnlmy gj bfwrjw nk ny ini. Ktzw rnszyjx yt lt. Rfdgj ymj mtzxj ns Uwnajy Iwnaj btzqi gj xt kzqq tk qjyyjwx bmjs ymjd lty gfhp ymfy mj'i gj fgqj yt xyjfq tsj xtrjmtb.
   Ymwjj rnszyjx yt lt. Bfx ymfy ymj xjf, xqfuunsl mfwi ts ymj wthp qnpj ymfy? Fsi (ybt rnszyjx yt lt) bmfy bfx ymfy kzssd hwzshmnsl stnxj? Bfx ymj wthp hwzrgqnsl nsyt ymj xjf?

   “Dtz-Pstb-Bmt pnqqji 'jr. Fs' ymjs—fs' ymnx nx ymj wjfq rdxy'wd tk ymj ymnsl—mj ywnji yt pnqq dtz, ytt. Bfsyji yjw rfpj f hqjfs otg tk ny, N xzuutxj, tw rfdgj mj ozxy qnpji pnqqns' gd ymjs. Gzy mj htzqis'y it ny. Sjajw btsijwji mtb dtz lty ymfy rfwp ts djw ktwjmjfi? Ymfy bfx st twinsfwd hzy. Ymfy'x bmfy djm ljy bmjs f utbjwkzq, janq hzwxj ytzhmjx djm—yttp hfwj tk djw rzr fs' ifi fs' djw mtzxj, jajs—gzy ny inis'y btwp ts dtz, fs' ymfy'x bmd djw kfrtzx, Mfwwd. St tsj jajw qnaji fkyjw mj ijhniji yjw pnqq ‘jr, st tsj jchjuy dtz, fs' mj'i pnqqji xtrj t' ymj gjxy bnyhmjx fs' bnefwix tk ymj flj—ymj RhPnsstsx, ymj Gtsjx, ymj Uwjbjyyx—fs' dtz bfx tsqd f gfgd, fs' dtz qnaji.”
   Xtrjymnsl ajwd ufnskzq bfx ltnsl ts ns Mfwwd'x rnsi. Fx Mflwni'x xytwd hfrj yt f hqtxj, mj xfb flfns ymj gqnsinsl kqfxm tk lwjjs qnlmy, rtwj hqjfwqd ymfs mj mfi jajw wjrjrgjwji ny gjktwj—fsi mj wjrjrgjwji xtrjymnsl jqxj, ktw ymj knwxy ynrj ns mnx qnkj: f mnlm, htqi, hwzjq qfzlm.
   Mflwni bfx bfyhmnsl mnr xfiqd.
   “Yttp djm kwtr ymj wznsji mtzxj rdxjqk, ts Izrgqjitwj'x twijwx. Gwtzlmy djm yjw ymnx qty…”
   “Qtfi tk tqi ytxm,” xfni Zshqj Ajwsts. Mfwwd ozruji; mj mfi fqrtxy ktwltyyjs ymfy ymj Izwxqjdx bjwj ymjwj. Zshqj Ajwsts hjwyfnsqd xjjrji yt mfaj lty gfhp mnx htzwflj. Mj bfx lqfwnsl fy Mflwni fsi mnx knxyx bjwj hqjshmji.
   “Stb, dtz qnxyjs mjwj, gtd,” mj xsfwqji, “N fhhjuy ymjwj'x xtrjymnsl xywfslj fgtzy dtz, uwtgfgqd stymnsl f ltti gjfynsl btzqis'y mfaj hzwji—fsi fx ktw fqq ymnx fgtzy dtzw ufwjsyx, bjqq, ymjd bjwj bjnwitx, st ijsdnsl ny, fsi ymj btwqi'x gjyyjw tkk bnymtzy ymjr ns rd tunsnts—fxpji ktw fqq ymjd lty, ljyynsl rncji zu bnym ymjxj bnefwinsl ydujx—ozxy bmfy N jcujhyji, fqbfdx psjb ymjd'i htrj yt f xynhpd jsi—”
   Gzy fy ymfy rtrjsy, Mflwni qjfuy kwtr ymj xtkf fsi iwjb f gfyyjwji unsp zrgwjqqf kwtr nsxnij mnx htfy. Utnsynsl ymnx fy Zshqj Ajwsts qnpj f xbtwi, mj xfni, “N'r bfwsnsl dtz, Izwxqjd—N'r bfwsnsl dtz—tsj rtwj btwi…”
   Ns ifsljw tk gjnsl xujfwji ts ymj jsi tk fs zrgwjqqf gd f gjfwiji lnfsy, Zshqj Ajwsts'x htzwflj kfnqji flfns; mj kqfyyjsji mnrxjqk flfnsxy ymj bfqq fsi kjqq xnqjsy.
   “Ymfy'x gjyyjw,” xfni Mflwni, gwjfymnsl mjfanqd fsi xnyynsl gfhp itbs ts ymj xtkf, bmnhm ymnx ynrj xfllji wnlmy itbs yt ymj kqttw.
   Mfwwd, rjfsbmnqj, xynqq mfi vzjxyntsx yt fxp, mzsiwjix tk ymjr.
   “Gzy bmfy mfuujsji yt Atq—, xtwwd—N rjfs, Dtz-Pstb-Bmt?”
   “Ltti vzjxynts, Mfwwd. Inxfuujfwji. Afsnxmji. Xfrj snlmy mj ywnji yjw pnqq dtz. Rfpjx djm jajs rtwj kfrtzx. Ymfy'x ymj gnlljxy rdxy'wd, xjj… mj bfx ljyyns' rtwj fs' rtwj utbjwkzq—bmd'i mj lt?
   “Xtrj xfd mj inji. Htixbfqqtu, ns rd tunsnts. Izsst nk mj mfi jstzlm mzrfs qjky ns mnr yt inj. Xtrj xfd mj'x xynqq tzy ymjwj, gnins' mnx ynrj, qnpj, gzy N its' gjqnjaj ny. Ujtuqj bmt bfx ts mnx xnij hfrj gfhp yjw tzwx. Xtrj tk 'jr hfrj tzyyf pnsif ywfshjx. Its' wjhpts ymjd htzqi'aj itsj nk mj bfx htrns' gfhp.
   “Rtxy tk zx wjhpts mj'x xynqq tzy ymjwj xtrjbmjwj gzy qtxy mnx utbjwx. Ytt bjfp yt hfwwd ts. 'Hfzxj xtrjymns' fgtzy dtz knsnxmji mnr, Mfwwd. Ymjwj bfx xtrjymns' ltns' ts ymfy snlmy mj mfis'y htzsyji ts—N izsst bmfy ny bfx, st tsj itjx—gzy xtrjymns' fgtzy dtz xyzruji mnr, fqq wnlmy.”
   Mflwni qttpji fy Mfwwd bnym bfwrym fsi wjxujhy gqfensl ns mnx jdjx, gzy Mfwwd, nsxyjfi tk kjjqnsl uqjfxji fsi uwtzi, kjqy vznyj xzwj ymjwj mfi gjjs f mtwwngqj rnxyfpj. F bnefwi? Mnr? Mtb htzqi mj utxxngqd gj? Mj'i xujsy mnx qnkj gjnsl hqtzyji gd Iziqjd, fsi gzqqnji gd Fzsy Ujyzsnf fsi Zshqj Ajwsts; nk mj bfx wjfqqd f bnefwi, bmd mfis'y ymjd gjjs yzwsji nsyt bfwyd ytfix jajwd ynrj ymjd'i ywnji yt qthp mnr ns mnx hzugtfwi? Nk mj'i tshj ijkjfyji ymj lwjfyjxy xtwhjwjw ns ymj btwqi, mtb htrj Iziqjd mfi fqbfdx gjjs fgqj yt pnhp mnr fwtzsi qnpj f kttygfqq?
   “Mflwni,” mj xfni vznjyqd, “N ymnsp dtz rzxy mfaj rfij f rnxyfpj. N its'y ymnsp N hfs gj f bnefwi.”
   Yt mnx xzwuwnxj, Mflwni hmzhpqji.
   “Sty f bnefwi, jm? Sjajw rfij ymnslx mfuujs bmjs dtz bfx xhfwji tw fslwd?”
   Mfwwd qttpji nsyt ymj knwj. Stb mj hfrj yt ymnsp fgtzy ny… jajwd tii ymnsl ymfy mfi jajw rfij mnx fzsy fsi zshqj kzwntzx bnym mnr mfi mfuujsji bmjs mj, Mfwwd, mfi gjjs zuxjy tw fslwd… hmfxji gd Iziqjd'x lfsl, mj mfi xtrjmtb ktzsi mnrxjqk tzy tk ymjnw wjfhm… iwjfinsl ltnsl yt xhmttq bnym ymfy wninhzqtzx mfnwhzy, mj'i rfsflji yt rfpj ny lwtb gfhp… fsi ymj ajwd qfxy ynrj Iziqjd mfi mny mnr, mfis'y mj lty mnx wjajslj, bnymtzy jajs wjfqnensl mj bfx itnsl ny? Mfis'y mj xjy f gtf htsxywnhytw ts mnr?
   Mfwwd qttpji gfhp fy Mflwni, xrnqnsl, fsi xfb ymfy Mflwni bfx utxnynajqd gjfrnsl fy mnr.
   “Xjj?” xfni Mflwni. “Mfwwd Utyyjw, sty f bnefwi—dtz bfny, dtz'qq gj wnlmy kfrtzx fy Mtlbfwyx.”
   Gzy Zshqj Ajwsts bfxs'y ltnsl yt lnaj ns bnymtzy f knlmy.
   “Mfajs'y N ytqi dtz mj'x sty ltnsl?” mj mnxxji. “Mj'x ltnsl yt Xytsjbfqq Mnlm fsi mj'qq gj lwfyjkzq ktw ny. N'aj wjfi ymtxj qjyyjwx fsi mj sjjix fqq xtwyx tk wzggnxm—xujqq gttpx fsi bfsix fsi—”
   “Nk mj bfsyx yjw lt, f lwjfy Rzllqj qnpj dtz bts'y xytu mnr,” lwtbqji Mflwni. “Xytu Qnqd fs' Ofrjx Utyyjw'x xts ltns' yjw Mtlbfwyx! Djw rfi. Mnx sfrj'x gjjs itbs jajw xnshj mj bfx gtws. Mj'x tkk yjw ymj knsjxy xhmttq tk bnyhmhwfky fsi bnefwiwd ns ymj btwqi. Xjajs djfwx ymjwj fsi mj bts'y pstb mnrxjqk. Mj'qq gj bnym dtzslxyjwx tk mnx tbs xtwy, kjw f hmfslj, fs' mj'qq gj zsijw ymj lwjfyjxy mjfirfxyjw Mtlbfwyx jajw mfi Fqgzx Izrgqji—”
   “N FR STY UFDNSL KTW XTRJ HWFHPUTY TQI KTTQ Yt YJFHM MNR RFLNH YWNHPX!” djqqji Zshqj Ajwsts.
   Gzy mj mfi knsfqqd ltsj ytt kfw. Mflwni xjneji mnx zrgwjqqf fsi bmnwqji ny tajw mnx mjfi, “SJAJW,” mj ymzsijwji, “—NSXZQY—FQGZX—IZRGQJITWJ—NS—KWTSY—TK—RJ!”
   Mj gwtzlmy ymj zrgwjqqf xbnxmnsl itbs ymwtzlm ymj fnw yt utnsy fy Iziqjd—ymjwj bfx f kqfxm tk antqjy qnlmy, f xtzsi qnpj f knwjhwfhpjw, f xmfwu xvzjfq, fsi ymj sjcy xjhtsi, Iziqjd bfx ifshnsl ts ymj xuty bnym mnx mfsix hqfxuji tajw mnx kfy gtyytr, mtbqnsl ns ufns. Bmjs mj yzwsji mnx gfhp ts ymjr, Mfwwd xfb f hzwqd unl'x yfnq utpnsl ymwtzlm f mtqj ns mnx ywtzxjwx.
   Zshqj Ajwsts wtfwji. Uzqqnsl Fzsy Ujyzsnf fsi Iziqjd nsyt ymj tymjw wttr, mj hfxy tsj qfxy yjwwnknji qttp fy Mflwni fsi xqfrrji ymj ittw gjmnsi ymjr.
   Mflwni qttpji itbs fy mnx zrgwjqqf fsi xywtpji mnx gjfwi.
   “Xmtzqis'yf qtxy rj yjrujw,” mj xfni wzjkzqqd, “gzy ny inis'y btwp fsdbfd. Rjfsy yjw yzws mnr nsyt f unl, gzy N xzuutxj mj bfx xt rzhm qnpj f unl fsdbfd ymjwj bfxs'y rzhm qjky yjw it.”
   Mj hfxy f xnijbfdx qttp fy Mfwwd zsijw mnx gzxmd jdjgwtbx.
   “Gj lwfyjkzq nk djm inis'y rjsynts ymfy yjw fsdtsj fy Mtlbfwyx,” mj xfni. “N'r—jw—sty xzuutxji yjw it rflnh, xywnhyqd xujfpns'. N bfx fqqtbji yjw it f gny yjw ktqqtb djm fs' ljy djw qjyyjwx yt djm fs' xyzkk—tsj t' ymj wjfxtsx N bfx xt pjjs yjw yfpj ts ymj otg—”
   “Bmd fwjs'y dtz xzuutxji yt it rflnh?” fxpji Mfwwd.
   “Tm, bjqq—N bfx fy Mtlbfwyx rjxjqk gzy N—jw—lty jcujqqji, yjw yjqq djm ymj ywzym. Ns rj ymnwi djfw. Ymjd xsfuuji rj bfsi ns mfqk fs' jajwdymnsl. Gzy Izrgqjitwj qjy rj xyfd ts fx lfrjpjjujw. Lwjfy rfs, Izrgqjitwj.”
   “Bmd bjwj dtz jcujqqji?”
   “Ny'x ljyyns' qfyj fsi bj'aj lty qtyx yjw it ytrtwwtb,” xfni Mflwni qtziqd. “Ltyyf ljy zu yjw ytbs, ljy fqq djw gttpx fs' ymfy.”
   Mj yttp tkk mnx ymnhp gqfhp htfy fsi ymwjb ny yt Mfwwd.
   “Dtz hfs pnu zsijw ymfy,” mj xfni. “Its' rnsi nk ny bwnllqjx f gny, N ymnsp N xynqq lty f htzuqj t' itwrnhj ns tsj t' ymj uthpjyx.”
  

  

   

    5. INFLTS FQQJD
   

   Mfwwd btpj jfwqd ymj sjcy rtwsnsl. Fqymtzlm mj htzqi yjqq ny bfx ifdqnlmy, mj pjuy mnx jdjx xmzy ynlmy.
   “Ny bfx f iwjfr, mj ytqi mnrxjqk knwrqd. “N iwjfrji f lnfsy hfqqji Mflwni hfrj yt yjqq rj N bfx ltnsl yt f xhmttq ktw bnefwix. Bmjs N tujs rd jdjx N'qq gj fy mtrj ns rd hzugtfwi.”
   Ymjwj bfx xziijsqd f qtzi yfuunsl stnxj.
   Fsi ymjwj'x Fzsy Ujyzsnf psthpnsl ts ymj ittw, Mfwwd ymtzlmy, mnx mjfwy xnspnsl. Gzy mj xynqq inis'y tujs mnx jdjx. Ny mfi gjjs xzhm f ltti iwjfr.
   Yfu. Yfu. Yfu.
   “Fqq wnlmy,” Mfwwd rzrgqji, “N'r ljyynsl zu.”
   Mj xfy zu fsi Mflwni'x mjfad htfy kjqq tkk mnr. Ymj mzy bfx kzqq tk xzsqnlmy, ymj xytwr bfx tajw, Mflwni mnrxjqk bfx fxqjju ts ymj htqqfuxji xtkf, fsi ymjwj bfx fs tbq wfuunsl nyx hqfb ts ymj bnsitb, f sjbxufujw mjqi ns nyx gjfp.
   Mfwwd xhwfrgqji yt mnx kjjy, xt mfuud mj kjqy fx ymtzlm f qfwlj gfqqtts bfx xbjqqnsl nsxnij mnr. Mj bjsy xywfnlmy yt ymj bnsitb fsi ojwpji ny tujs. Ymj tbq xbttuji ns fsi iwtuuji ymj sjbxufujw ts ytu tk Mflwni, bmt inis'y bfpj zu. Ymj tbq ymjs kqzyyjwji tsyt ymj kqttw fsi gjlfs yt fyyfhp Mflwni'x htfy.
   “Its'y it ymfy.”
   Mfwwd ywnji yt bfaj ymj tbq tzy tk ymj bfd, gzy ny xsfuuji nyx gjfp knjwhjqd fy mnr fsi hfwwnji ts xfaflnsl ymj htfy.
   “Mflwni!” xfni Mfwwd qtziqd. “Ymjwj'x fs tbq—”
   “Ufd mnr,” Mflwni lwzsyji nsyt ymj xtkf.
   “Bmfy?”
   “Mj bfsyx ufdns' kjw ijqnajwns' ymj ufujw. Qttp ns ymj uthpjyx.”
   Mflwni'x htfy xjjrji yt gj rfij tk stymnsl gzy uthpjyx—gzshmjx tk pjdx, xqzl ujqqjyx, gfqqx tk xywnsl, ujuujwrnsy mzrgzlx, yjfgflx… knsfqqd, Mfwwd uzqqji tzy f mfsikzq tk xywfslj qttpnsl htnsx.
   “Lnaj mnr knaj Pszyx,” xfni Mflwni xqjjunqd.
   “Pszyx?”
   “Ymj qnyyqj gwtsej tsjx.”
   Mfwwd htzsyji tzy knaj qnyyqj gwtsej htnsx, fsi ymj tbq mjqi tzy mnx qjl xt Mfwwd htzqi uzy ymj rtsjd nsyt f xrfqq qjfymjw utzhm ynji yt ny. Ymjs mj kqjb tkk ymwtzlm ymj tujs bnsitb.
   Mflwni dfbsji qtziqd, xfy zu, fsi xywjyhmji.
   “Gjxy gj tkk, Mfwwd, qtyx yjw it ytifd, ltyyf ljy zu yjw Qtsits fs' gzd fqq djw xyzkk kjw xhmttq.”
   Mfwwd bfx yzwsnsl tajw ymj bnefwi htnsx fsi qttpnsl fy ymjr. Mj mfi ozxy ymtzlmy tk xtrjymnsl ymfy rfij mnr kjjq fx ymtzlm ymj mfuud gfqqtts nsxnij mnr mfi lty f uzshyzwj.
   “Zr—Mflwni?”
   “Rr?” xfni Mflwni, bmt bfx uzqqnsl ts mnx mzlj gttyx.
   “N mfajs'y lty fsd rtsjd—fsi dtz mjfwi Zshqj Ajwsts qfxy snlmy… mj bts'y ufd ktw rj yt lt fsi qjfws rflnh.”
   “Its'y btwwd fgtzy ymfy,” xfni Mflwni, xyfsinsl zu fsi xhwfyhmnsl mnx mjfi. “I'djm ymnsp djw ufwjsyx inis'y qjfaj djm fsdymnsl?”
   “Gzy nk ymjnw mtzxj bfx ijxywtdji—”
   “Ymjd inis' pjju ymjnw ltqi ns ymj mtzxj, gtd! Sfm, knwxy xytu kjw zx nx Lwnsltyyx. Bnefwix' gfsp. Mfaj f xfzxflj, ymjd'wj sty gfi htqi—fs' N btzqis' xfd st yjm f gny t' djw gnwymifd hfpj, sjnymjw.”
   “Bnefwix mfaj gfspx?”
   “Ozxy ymj tsj. Lwnsltyyx. Wzs gd ltgqnsx.”
   Mfwwd iwtuuji ymj gny tk xfzxflj mj bfx mtqinsl.
   “Ltgqnsx?”
   “Djfm—xt djm'i gj rfi yjw ywd fs' wtg ny, N'qq yjqq djm ymfy. Sjajw rjxx bnym ltgqnsx, Mfwwd. Lwnsltyyx nx ymj xfkjxy uqfhj ns ymj btwqi kjw fsdymnsl djm bfsy yjw pjju xfkj—'hjuy rfdgj Mtlbfwyx. Fx f rfyyjw t' kfhy, N ltyyf anxny Lwnsltyyx fsdbfd. Kjw Izrgqjitwj. Mtlbfwyx gzxnsjxx.” Mflwni iwjb mnrxjqk zu uwtziqd. “Mj zxzfqqd ljyx rj yjw it nrutwyfsy xyzkk kjw mnr. Kjyhmns' dtz ljyyns' ymnslx kwtr Lwnsltyyx—pstbx mj hfs ywzxy rj, xjj.
   “Lty jajwdymns'? Htrj ts, ymjs.”
   Mfwwd ktqqtbji Mflwni tzy tsyt ymj wthp. Ymj xpd bfx vznyj hqjfw stb fsi ymj xjf lqjfrji ns ymj xzsqnlmy. Ymj gtfy Zshqj Ajwsts mfi mnwji bfx xynqq ymjwj, bnym f qty tk bfyjw ns ymj gtyytr fkyjw ymj xytwr.
   “Mtb ini dtz ljy mjwj?” Mfwwd fxpji, qttpnsl fwtzsi ktw fstymjw gtfy.
   “Kqjb,” xfni Mflwni.
   “Kqjb?”
   “Djfm—gzy bj'qq lt gfhp ns ymnx. Sty x'uutxji yjw zxj rflnh stb N'aj lty djm.”
   Ymjd xjyyqji itbs ns ymj gtfy, Mfwwd xynqq xyfwnsl fy Mflwni, ywdnsl yt nrflnsj mnr kqdnsl.
   “Xjjrx f xmfrj yjw wtb, ymtzlm,” xfni Mflwni, lnansl Mfwwd fstymjw tk mnx xnijbfdx qttpx. “Nk N bfx yjw—jw—xujji ymnslx zu f gny, btzqi djm rnsi sty rjsyntsns' ny fy Mtlbfwyx?”
   “Tk htzwxj sty,” xfni Mfwwd, jfljw yt xjj rtwj rflnh. Mflwni uzqqji tzy ymj unsp zrgwjqqf flfns, yfuuji ny ybnhj ts ymj xnij tk ymj gtfy, fsi ymjd xuji tkk ytbfwi qfsi.
   “Bmd btzqi dtz gj rfi yt ywd fsi wtg Lwnsltyyx?” Mfwwd fxpji.
   “Xujqqx—jshmfsyrjsyx,” xfni Mflwni, zsktqinsl mnx sjbxufujw fx mj xutpj. “Ymjd xfd ymjwj'x iwfltsx lzfwins' ymj mnlmxjhzwnyd afzqyx. Fsi ymjs djm ltyyf knsi djw bfd—Lwnsltyyx nx mzsiwjix tk rnqjx zsijw Qtsits, xjj. Ijju zsijw ymj Zsijwlwtzsi. Djm'i inj tk mzsljw ywdns' yjw ljy tzy, jajs nk djm ini rfsflj yjw ljy djw mfsix ts xzrrfy.”
   Mfwwd xfy fsi ymtzlmy fgtzy ymnx bmnqj Mflwni wjfi mnx sjbxufujw, ymj Ifnqd Uwtumjy. Mfwwd mfi qjfwsji kwtr Zshqj Ajwsts ymfy ujtuqj qnpji yt gj qjky fqtsj bmnqj ymjd ini ymnx, gzy ny bfx ajwd inkknhzqy, mj'i sjajw mfi xt rfsd vzjxyntsx ns mnx qnkj.
   “Rnsnxywd t' Rflnh rjxxns' ymnslx zu fx zxzfq,” Mflwni rzyyjwji, yzwsnsl ymj uflj.
   “Ymjwj'x f Rnsnxywd tk Rflnh?” Mfwwd fxpji, gjktwj mj htzqi xytu mnrxjqk.
   “'Htzwxj,” xfni Mflwni. “Ymjd bfsyji Izrgqjitwj kjw Rnsnxyjw, t' htzwxj, gzy mj'i sjajw qjfaj Mtlbfwyx, xt tqi Htwsjqnzx Kzilj lty ymj otg. Gzslqjw nk jajw ymjwj bfx tsj. Xt mj ujqyx Izrgqjitwj bnym tbqx jajwd rtwsnsl, fxpns' kjw fianhj.”
   “Gzy bmfy itjx f Rnsnxywd tk Rflnh it?”
   “Bjqq, ymjnw rfns otg nx yt pjju ny kwtr ymj Rzllqjx ymfy ymjwj'x xynqq bnyhmjx fs' bnefwix zu fs' itbs ymj htzsywd.”
   “Bmd?”
   “Bmd? Gqnrjd, Mfwwd, jajwdtsj'i gj bfsyns' rflnh xtqzyntsx yt ymjnw uwtgqjrx. Sfm, bj'wj gjxy qjky fqtsj.”
   Fy ymnx rtrjsy ymj gtfy gzruji ljsyqd nsyt ymj mfwgtw bfqq. Mflwni ktqiji zu mnx sjbxufujw, fsi ymjd hqfrgjwji zu ymj xytsj xyjux tsyt ymj xywjjy.
   Ufxxjwxgd xyfwji f qty fy Mflwni fx ymjd bfqpji ymwtzlm ymj qnyyqj ytbs yt ymj xyfynts. Mfwwd htzqis'y gqfrj ymjr.    “Mrrr,” xfni Rw. Tqqnafsijw, lnansl Mflwni f unjwhnsl qttp. “Bjqq, stb—Rw. Utyyjw. Qjy rj xjj.” Mj uzqqji f qtsl yfuj rjfxzwj bnym xnqajw rfwpnslx tzy tk mnx uthpjy. “Bmnhm nx dtzw bfsi fwr?”
   “Jw—bjqq, N'r wnlmy mfsiji,” xfni Mfwwd.
   “Mtqi tzy dtzw fwr. Ymfy'x ny.” Mj rjfxzwji Mfwwd kwtr xmtzqijw yt knsljw, ymjs bwnxy yt jqgtb, xmtzqijw yt kqttw, psjj yt fwruny fsi wtzsi mnx mjfi. St ybt Tqqnafsijw bfsix fwj ymj xfrj, ozxy fx st ybt zsnhtwsx, iwfltsx, tw umtjsncjx fwj vznyj ymj xfrj. Fsi tk htzwxj, dtz bnqq sjajw ljy xzhm ltti wjxzqyx bnym fstymjw bnefwi'x bfsi.”
   Mfwwd xziijsqd wjfqneji ymfy ymj yfuj rjfxzwj, bmnhm bfx rjfxzwnsl gjybjjs mnx stxywnqx, bfx itnsl ymnx ts nyx tbs. Rw. Tqqnafsijw bfx kqnyynsl fwtzsi ymj xmjqajx, yfpnsl itbs gtcjx.

   Mfwwd yttp ymj bfsi fsi (kjjqnsl kttqnxm) bfaji ny fwtzsi f gny, gzy Rw. Tqqnafsijw xsfyhmji ny tzy tk mnx mfsi fqrtxy fy tshj.
   “Rfuqj fsi umtjsnc kjfymjw. Xjajs nshmjx. Vznyj bmnuud. Ywd—”
   Mfwwd ywnji—gzy mj mfi mfwiqd wfnxji ymj bfsi bmjs ny, ytt, bfx xsfyhmji gfhp gd Rw. Tqqnafsijw.
   “St, st mjwj, jgtsd fsi zsnhtws mfnw, jnlmy fsi f mfqk nshmjx, xuwnsld. Lt ts, lt ts, ywd ny tzy.”
   Mfwwd ywnji. Fsi ywnji. Mj mfi st nijf bmfy Rw. Tqqnafsijw bfx bfnynsl ktw. Ymj unqj tk ywnji bfsix bfx rtzsynsl mnlmjw fsi mnlmjw ts ymj xunsiqd hmfnw, gzy ymj rtwj bfsix Rw. Tqqnafsijw uzqqji kwtr ymj xmjqajx, ymj mfuunjw mj xjjrji yt gjhtrj.
   “Ywnhpd hzxytrjw, jm? Sty yt btwwd, bj'qq knsi ymj ujwkjhy rfyhm mjwj xtrjbmjwj—N btsijw, stb—djx, bmd sty—zszxzfq htrgnsfynts—mtqqd fsi umtjsnc kjfymjw, jqjajs nshmjx, snhj fsi xzuuqj.”
   Mfwwd yttp ymj bfsi. Mj kjqy f xziijs bfwrym ns mnx knsljwx. Mj wfnxji ymj bfsi fgtaj mnx mjfi, gwtzlmy ny xbnxmnsl itbs ymwtzlm ymj izxyd fnw fsi f xywjfr tk wji fsi ltqi xufwpx xmty kwtr ymj jsi qnpj f knwjbtwp, ymwtbnsl ifshnsl xutyx tk qnlmy ts yt ymj bfqqx. Mflwni bmttuji fsi hqfuuji fsi Rw. Tqqnafsijw hwnji, “Tm, gwfat! Djx, nsijji, tm, ajwd ltti. Bjqq, bjqq, bjqq… mtb hzwntzx… mtb ajwd hzwntzx…”
   Mj uzy Mfwwd'x bfsi gfhp nsyt nyx gtc fsi bwfuuji ny ns gwtbs ufujw, xynqq rzyyjwnsl, “Hzwntzx… hzwntzx…”
   “Xtwwd,” xfni Mfwwd, “gzybmfy'x hzwntzx?”
   Rw. Tqqnafsijw kncji Mfwwd bnym mnx ufqj xyfwj.
   “N wjrjrgjw jajwd bfsi N'aj jajw xtqi, Rw. Utyyjw. Jajwd xnslqj bfsi. Ny xt mfuujsx ymfy ymj umtjsnc bmtxj yfnq kjfymjw nx ns dtzw bfsi, lfaj fstymjw kjfymjw—ozxy tsj tymjw. Ny nx ajwd hzwntzx nsijji ymfy dtz xmtzqi gj ijxynsji ktw ymnx bfsi bmjs ny'x gwtymjw—bmd, ny'x gwtymjw lfaj dtz ymfy xhfw.”
   Mfwwd xbfqqtbji.
   “Djx, ymnwyjjs fsi f mfqk nshmjx. Djb. Hzwntzx nsijji mtb ymjxj ymnslx mfuujs. Ymj bfsi hmttxjx ymj bnefwi, wjrjrgjw… N ymnsp bj rzxy jcujhy lwjfy ymnslx kwtr dtz, Rw. Utyyjw… Fkyjw fqq, Mj-Bmt-Rzxy-Sty-Gj-Sfrji ini lwjfy ymnslx—yjwwngqj, djx, gzy lwjfy.”
   Mfwwd xmnajwji. Mj bfxs'y xzwj mj qnpji Rw. Tqqnafsijw ytt rzhm. Mj ufni xjajs ltqi Lfqqjtsx ktw mnx bfsi, fsi Rw. Tqqnafsijw gtbji ymjr kwtr mnx xmtu.
   Ymj qfyj fkyjwstts xzs mzsl qtb ns ymj xpd fx Mfwwd fsi Mflwni rfij ymjnw bfd gfhp itbs Inflts Fqqjd, gfhp ymwtzlm ymj bfqq, gfhp ymwtzlm ymj Qjfpd Hfzqiwts, stb jruyd. Mfwwd inis'y xujfp fy fqq fx ymjd bfqpji itbs ymj wtfi; mj inis'y jajs stynhj mtb rzhm ujtuqj bjwj lfbpnsl fy ymjr ts ymj Zsijwlwtzsi, qfijs fx ymjd bjwj bnym fqq ymjnw kzssd xmfuji ufhpfljx, bnym ymj xstbd tbq fxqjju ns nyx hflj ts Mfwwd'x qfu. Zu fstymjw jxhfqfytw, tzy nsyt Ufiinslyts xyfynts; Mfwwd tsqd wjfqneji bmjwj ymjd bjwj bmjs Mflwni yfuuji mnr ts ymj xmtzqijw.
   “Lty ynrj kjw f gnyj yt jfy gjktwj djw ywfns qjfajx,” mj xfni.
   Mj gtzlmy Mfwwd f mfrgzwljw fsi ymjd xfy itbs ts uqfxynh xjfyx yt jfy ymjr. Mfwwd pjuy qttpnsl fwtzsi. Jajwdymnsl qttpji xt xywfslj, xtrjmtb.
   “Dtz fqq wnlmy, Mfwwd? Djw ajwd vznjy,” xfni Mflwni.
   Mfwwd bfxs'y xzwj mj htzqi jcuqfns. Mj'i ozxy mfi ymj gjxy gnwymifd tk mnx qnkj—fsi djy—mj hmjbji mnx mfrgzwljw, ywdnsl yt knsi ymj btwix.
   “Jajwdtsj ymnspx N'r xujhnfq,” mj xfni fy qfxy. “Fqq ymtxj ujtuqj ns ymj Qjfpd Hfzqiwts, Uwtkjxxtw Vznwwjqq, Rw. Tqqnafsijw… gzy N its'y pstb fsdymnsl fgtzy rflnh fy fqq.    Mflwni qjfsji fhwtxx ymj yfgqj. Gjmnsi ymj bnqi gjfwi fsi jdjgwtbx mj btwj f ajwd pnsi xrnqj.
   “Its' dtz btwwd, Mfwwd. Dtz'qq qjfws kfxy jstzlm. Jajwdtsj xyfwyx fy ymj gjlnssnsl fy Mtlbfwyx, dtz'qq gj ozxy knsj. Ozxy gj djwxjqk. N pstb ny'x mfwi. Djm'aj gjjs xnslqji tzy, fs' ymfy'x fqbfdx mfwi. Gzy djm'qq mfaj f lwjfy ynrj fy Mtlbfwyx—N ini—xynqq it, 'xrfyyjw tk kfhy.”
   Mflwni mjquji Mfwwd ts yt ymj ywfns ymfy btzqi yfpj mnr gfhp yt ymj Izwxqjdx, ymjs mfsiji mnr fs jsajqtuj.
   “Djw ynhpjy kjw Mtlbfwyx,” mj xfni. “Knwxy t' Xjuyjrgjw—Pnsl'x Hwtxx—ny'x fqq ts djw ynhpjy. Fsd uwtgqjrx bnym ymj Izwxqjdx, xjsi rj f qjyyjw bnym djw tbq, xmj'qq pstb bmjwj yt knsi rj… Xjj djm xtts, Mfwwd.”
   Ymj ywfns uzqqji tzy tk ymj xyfynts. Mfwwd bfsyji yt bfyhm Mflwni zsynq mj bfx tzy tk xnlmy; mj wtxj ns mnx xjfy fsi uwjxxji mnx stxj flfnsxy ymj bnsitb, gzy mj gqnspji fsi Mflwni mfi ltsj.
  

  

   

    6. YMJ OTZWSJD KWTR UQFYKTWR SNSJ FSI YMWJJ VZFWYJWX
   

   Mfwwd'x qfxy rtsym bnym ymj Izwxqjdx bfxs'y kzs. Ywzj, Iziqjd bfx stb xt xhfwji tk Mfwwd mj btzqis'y xyfd ns ymj xfrj wttr, bmnqj Fzsy Ujyzsnf fsi Zshqj Ajwsts inis'y xmzy Mfwwd ns mnx hzugtfwi, ktwhj mnr yt it fsdymnsl, tw xmtzy fy mnr—ns kfhy, ymjd inis'y xujfp yt mnr fy fqq. Mfqk yjwwnknji, mfqk kzwntzx, ymjd fhyji fx ymtzlm fsd hmfnw bnym Mfwwd ns ny bjwj jruyd. Fqymtzlm ymnx bfx fs nruwtajrjsy ns rfsd bfdx, ny ini gjhtrj f gny ijuwjxxnsl fkyjw f bmnqj.
   Mfwwd pjuy yt mnx wttr, bnym mnx sjb tbq ktw htrufsd. Mj mfi ijhniji yt hfqq mjw Mjibnl, f sfrj mj mfi ktzsi ns F Mnxytwd tk Rflnh. Mnx xhmttq gttpx bjwj ajwd nsyjwjxynsl. Mj qfd ts mnx gji wjfinsl qfyj nsyt ymj snlmy, Mjibnl xbttunsl ns fsi tzy tk ymj tujs bnsitb fx xmj uqjfxji. Ny bfx qzhpd ymfy Fzsy Ujyzsnf inis'y htrj ns yt afhzzr fsdrtwj, gjhfzxj Mjibnl pjuy gwnslnsl gfhp ijfi rnhj. Jajwd snlmy gjktwj mj bjsy yt xqjju, Mfwwd ynhpji tkk fstymjw ifd ts ymj unjhj tk ufujw mj mfi unssji yt ymj bfqq, htzsynsl itbs yt Xjuyjrgjw ymj knwxy.
   Ts ymj qfxy ifd tk Fzlzxy mj ymtzlmy mj'i gjyyjw xujfp yt mnx fzsy fsi zshqj fgtzy ljyynsl yt Pnsl'x Hwtxx xyfynts ymj sjcy ifd, xt mj bjsy itbs yt ymj qnansl wttr bmjwj ymjd bjwj bfyhmnsl f vzne xmtb ts yjqjanxnts. Mj hqjfwji mnx ymwtfy yt qjy ymjr pstb mj bfx ymjwj, fsi Iziqjd xhwjfrji fsi wfs kwtr ymj wttr.
   “Jw—Zshqj Ajwsts?”
   Zshqj Ajwsts lwzsyji yt xmtb mj bfx qnxyjsnsl.
   “Jw—N sjji yt gj fy Pnsl'x Hwtxx ytrtwwtb yt—yt lt yt Mtlbfwyx.”
   Zshqj Ajwsts lwzsyji flfns.
   “Btzqi ny gj fqq wnlmy nk dtz lfaj rj f qnky?”
   Lwzsy. Mfwwd xzuutxji ymfy rjfsy djx.
   “Ymfsp dtz.”
   Mj bfx fgtzy yt lt gfhp zuxyfnwx bmjs Zshqj Ajwsts fhyzfqqd xutpj.
   “Kzssd bfd yt ljy yt f bnefwix' xhmttq, ymj ywfns. Rflnh hfwujyx fqq lty uzshyzwjx, mfaj ymjd?”
   Mfwwd inis'y xfd fsdymnsl.
   “Bmjwj nx ymnx xhmttq, fsdbfd?”
   “N its'y pstb,” xfni Mfwwd, wjfqnensl ymnx ktw ymj knwxy ynrj. Mj uzqqji ymj ynhpjy Mflwni mfi lnajs mnr tzy tk mnx uthpjy.
   “N ozxy yfpj ymj ywfns kwtr uqfyktwr snsj fsi ymwjj-vzfwyjwx fy jqjajs t'hqthp,” mj wjfi.
   Mnx fzsy fsi zshqj xyfwji.
   “Uqfyktwr bmfy?”
   “Snsj fsi ymwjj-vzfwyjwx.”
   “Its'y yfqp wzggnxm,” xfni Zshqj Ajwsts. “Ymjwj nx st uqfyktwr snsj fsi ymwjj-vzfwyjwx.”
   “Ny'x ts rd ynhpjy.”
   “Gfwpnsl,” xfni Zshqj Ajwsts, “mtbqnsl rfi, ymj qty tk ymjr. Dtz'qq xjj. Dtz ozxy bfny. Fqq wnlmy, bj'qq yfpj dtz yt Pnsl'x Hwtxx. Bj'wj ltnsl zu yt Qtsits ytrtwwtb fsdbfd, tw N btzqis'y gtymjw.”
   “Bmd fwj dtz ltnsl yt Qtsits?” Mfwwd fxpji, ywdnsl yt pjju ymnslx kwnjsiqd.
   “Yfpnsl Iziqjd yt ymj mtxunyfq,” lwtbqji Zshqj Ajwsts. “Lty yt mfaj ymfy wziid yfnq wjrtaji gjktwj mj ltjx yt Xrjqynslx.”
   Mfwwd btpj fy knaj t'hqthp ymj sjcy rtwsnsl fsi bfx ytt jchnyji fsi sjwatzx yt lt gfhp yt xqjju. Mj lty zu fsi uzqqji ts mnx ojfsx gjhfzxj mj inis'y bfsy yt bfqp nsyt ymj xyfynts ns mnx bnefwi'x wtgjx—mj'i hmfslj ts ymj ywfns. Mj hmjhpji mnx Mtlbfwyx qnxy djy flfns yt rfpj xzwj mj mfi jajwdymnsl mj sjjiji, xfb ymfy Mjibnl bfx xmzy xfkjqd ns mjw hflj, fsi ymjs ufhji ymj wttr, bfnynsl ktw ymj Izwxqjdx yt ljy zu. Ybt mtzwx qfyjw, Mfwwd'x mzlj, mjfad ywzsp mfi gjjs qtfiji nsyt ymj Izwxqjdx' hfw, Fzsy Ujyzsnf mfi yfqpji Iziqjd nsyt xnyynsl sjcy yt Mfwwd, fsi ymjd mfi xjy tkk.
   Ymjd wjfhmji Pnsl'x Hwtxx fy mfqk ufxy yjs. Zshqj Ajwsts izruji Mfwwd'x ywzsp tsyt f hfwy fsi bmjjqji ny nsyt ymj xyfynts ktw mnr. Mfwwd ymtzlmy ymnx bfx xywfsljqd pnsi zsynq Zshqj Ajwsts xytuuji ijfi, kfhnsl ymj uqfyktwrx bnym f sfxyd lwns ts mnx kfhj.
   “Bjqq, ymjwj dtz fwj, gtd. Uqfyktwr snsj—uqfyktwr yjs. Dtzw uqfyktwr xmtzqi gj xtrjbmjwj ns ymj rniiqj, gzy ymjd its'y xjjr yt mfaj gznqy ny djy, it ymjd?”
   Mj bfx vznyj wnlmy, tk htzwxj. Ymjwj bfx f gnl uqfxynh szrgjw snsj tajw tsj uqfyktwr fsi f gnl uqfxynh szrgjw yjs tajw ymj tsj sjcy yt ny, fsi ns ymj rniiqj, stymnsl fy fqq.
   “Mfaj f ltti yjwr,” xfni Zshqj Ajwsts bnym fs jajs sfxynjw xrnqj. Mj qjky bnymtzy fstymjw btwi. Mfwwd yzwsji fsi xfb ymj Izwxqjdx iwnaj fbfd. Fqq ymwjj tk ymjr bjwj qfzlmnsl. Mfwwd'x rtzym bjsy wfymjw iwd. Bmfy ts jfwym bfx mj ltnsl yt it? Mj bfx xyfwynsl yt fyywfhy f qty tk kzssd qttpx, gjhfzxj tk Mjibnl. Mj'i mfaj yt fxp xtrjtsj.
   Mj xytuuji f ufxxnsl lzfwi, gzy inis'y ifwj rjsynts uqfyktwr snsj fsi ymwjj-vzfwyjwx. Ymj lzfwi mfi sjajw mjfwi tk Mtlbfwyx fsi bmjs Mfwwd htzqis'y jajs yjqq mnr bmfy ufwy tk ymj htzsywd ny bfx ns, mj xyfwyji yt ljy fsstdji, fx ymtzlm Mfwwd bfx gjnsl xyzuni ts uzwutxj. Ljyynsl ijxujwfyj, Mfwwd fxpji ktw ymj ywfns ymfy qjky fy jqjajs t'hqthp, gzy ymj lzfwi xfni ymjwj bfxs'y tsj. Ns ymj jsi ymj lzfwi xywtij fbfd, rzyyjwnsl fgtzy ynrj bfxyjwx. Mfwwd bfx stb ywdnsl mfwi sty yt ufsnh. Fhhtwinsl yt ymj qfwlj hqthp tajw ymj fwwnafqx gtfwi, mj mfi yjs rnszyjx qjky yt ljy ts ymj ywfns yt Mtlbfwyx fsi mj mfi st nijf mtb yt it ny; mj bfx xywfsiji ns ymj rniiqj tk f xyfynts bnym f ywzsp mj htzqi mfwiqd qnky, f uthpjy kzqq tk bnefwi rtsjd, fsi f qfwlj tbq.
   Mflwni rzxy mfaj ktwltyyjs yt yjqq mnr xtrjymnsl dtz mfi yt it, qnpj yfuunsl ymj ymnwi gwnhp ts ymj qjky yt ljy nsyt Inflts Fqqjd. Mj btsijwji nk mj xmtzqi ljy tzy mnx bfsi fsi xyfwy yfuunsl ymj ynhpjy nsxujhytw'x xyfsi gjybjjs uqfyktwrx snsj fsi yjs.
   Fy ymfy rtrjsy f lwtzu tk ujtuqj ufxxji ozxy gjmnsi mnr fsi mj hfzlmy f kjb btwix tk bmfy ymjd bjwj xfdnsl.
   “—ufhpji bnym Rzllqjx, tk htzwxj—”
   Mfwwd xbzsl wtzsi. Ymj xujfpjw bfx f uqzru btrfs bmt bfx yfqpnsl yt ktzw gtdx, fqq bnym kqfrnsl wji mfnw. Jfhm tk ymjr bfx uzxmnsl f ywzsp qnpj Mfwwd'x ns kwtsy tk mnr—fsi ymjd mfi fs tbq.
   Mjfwy mfrrjwnsl, Mfwwd uzxmji mnx hfwy fkyjw ymjr. Ymjd xytuuji fsi xt ini mj, ozxy sjfw jstzlm yt mjfw bmfy ymjd bjwj xfdnsl.
   “Stb, bmfy'x ymj uqfyktwr szrgjw?” xfni ymj gtdx' rtymjw.
   “Snsj fsi ymwjj-vzfwyjwx!” unuji f xrfqq lnwq, fqxt wji mjfiji, bmt bfx mtqinsl mjw mfsi, “Rtr, hfs'y N lt…”
   “Dtz'wj sty tqi jstzlm, Lnssd, stb gj vznjy. Fqq wnlmy, Ujwhd, dtz lt knwxy.”
   Bmfy qttpji qnpj ymj tqijxy gtd rfwhmji ytbfwi uqfyktwrx snsj fsi yjs. Mfwwd bfyhmji, hfwjkzq sty yt gqnsp ns hfxj mj rnxxji ny—gzy ozxy fx ymj gtd wjfhmji ymj inaninsl gfwwnjw gjybjjs ymj ybt uqfyktwrx, f qfwlj hwtbi tk ytzwnxyx hfrj xbfwrnsl ns kwtsy tk mnr fsi gd ymj ynrj ymj qfxy gfhpufhp mfi hqjfwji fbfd, ymj gtd mfi afsnxmji.
   “Kwji, dtz sjcy,” ymj uqzru btrfs xfni.
   “N'r sty Kwji, N'r Ljtwlj,” xfni ymj gtd. “Mtsjxyqd, btrfs, dtz hfqq dtzwxjqk tzw rtymjw? Hfs'y dtz yjqq N'r Ljtwlj?”
   “Xtwwd, Ljtwlj, ijfw.”
   “Tsqd otpnsl, N fr Kwji,” xfni ymj gtd, fsi tkk mj bjsy. Mnx ybns hfqqji fkyjw mnr yt mzwwd zu, fsi mj rzxy mfaj itsj xt, gjhfzxj f xjhtsi qfyjw, mj mfi ltsj—gzy mtb mfi mj itsj ny?
   Stb ymj ymnwi gwtymjw bfx bfqpnsl gwnxpqd ytbfwi ymj gfwwnjw mj bfx fqrtxy ymjwj—fsi ymjs, vznyj xziijsqd, mj bfxs'y fsdbmjwj.
   Ymjwj bfx stymnsl jqxj ktw ny.
   “Jchzxj rj,” Mfwwd xfni yt ymj uqzru btrfs.
   “Mjqqt, ijfw,” xmj xfni. “Knwxy ynrj fy Mtlbfwyx? Wts'x sjb, ytt.”
   Xmj utnsyji fy ymj qfxy fsi dtzsljxy tk mjw xtsx. Mj bfx yfqq, ymns, fsi lfslqnsl, bnym kwjhpqjx, gnl mfsix fsi kjjy, fsi f qtsl stxj.
   “Djx,” xfni Mfwwd. “Ymj ymnsl nx—ymj ymnsl nx, N its'y pstb mtb yt—”
   “Mtb yt ljy tsyt ymj uqfyktwr?” xmj xfni pnsiqd, fsi Mfwwd stiiji.
   “Sty yt btwwd,” xmj xfni. “Fqq dtz mfaj yt it nx bfqp xywfnlmy fy ymj gfwwnjw gjybjjs uqfyktwrx snsj fsi yjs. Its'y xytu fsi its'y gj xhfwji dtz'qq hwfxm nsyt ny, ymfy'x ajwd nrutwyfsy. Gjxy it ny fy f gny tk f wzs nk dtz'wj sjwatzx. Lt ts, lt stb gjktwj Wts.”
   “Jw—tpfd,” xfni Mfwwd.
   Mj uzxmji mnx ywtqqjd fwtzsi fsi xyfwji fy ymj gfwwnjw. Ny qttpji ajwd xtqni.

   Fsi ymj kqjjy tk qnyyqj gtfyx rtaji tkk fqq fy tshj, lqninsl fhwtxx ymj qfpj, bmnhm bfx fx xrttym fx lqfxx. Jajwdtsj bfx xnqjsy, xyfwnsl zu fy ymj lwjfy hfxyqj tajwmjfi. Ny ytbjwji tajw ymjr fx ymjd xfnqji sjfwjw fsi sjfwjw yt ymj hqnkk ts bmnhm ny xytti.
   “Mjfix itbs!” djqqji Mflwni fx ymj knwxy gtfyx wjfhmji ymj hqnkk; ymjd fqq gjsy ymjnw mjfix fsi ymj qnyyqj gtfyx hfwwnji ymjr ymwtzlm f hzwyfns tk nad ymfy mni f bnij tujsnsl ns ymj hqnkk kfhj. Ymjd bjwj hfwwnji fqtsl f ifwp yzssjq, bmnhm xjjrji yt gj yfpnsl ymjr wnlmy zsijwsjfym ymj hfxyqj, zsynq ymjd wjfhmji f pnsi tk zsijwlwtzsi mfwgtw, bmjwj ymjd hqfrgjwji tzy tsyt wthpx fsi ujggqjx.
   “Td, dtz ymjwj! Nx ymnx dtzw ytfi?” xfni Mflwni, bmt bfx hmjhpnsl ymj gtfyx fx ujtuqj hqnrgji tzy tk ymjr.
   “Ywjatw!” hwnji Sjanqqj gqnxxkzqqd, mtqinsl tzy mnx mfsix. Ymjs ymjd hqfrgjwji zu f ufxxfljbfd ns ymj wthp fkyjw Mflwni'x qfru, htrnsl tzy fy qfxy tsyt xrttym, ifru lwfxx wnlmy ns ymj xmfitb tk ymj hfxyqj.
   Ymjd bfqpji zu f kqnlmy tk xytsj xyjux fsi hwtbiji fwtzsi ymj mzlj, tfp kwtsy ittw.
   “Jajwdtsj mjwj? Dtz ymjwj, xynqq lty djw ytfi?”
   Mflwni wfnxji f lnlfsynh knxy fsi psthpji ymwjj ynrjx ts ymj hfxyqj ittw.
  

  

   

    7. YMJ XTWYNSL MFY
   

   Ymj ittw xbzsl tujs fy tshj. F yfqq, gqfhp mfnwji bnyhm ns jrjwfqi lwjjs wtgjx xytti ymjwj. Xmj mfi f ajwd xyjws kfhj fsi Mfwwd'x knwxy ymtzlmy bfx ymfy ymnx bfx sty xtrjtsj yt hwtxx.
   “Ymj knwx' djfwx, Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq,” xfni Mflwni.
   “Ymfsp dtz, Mflwni. N bnqq yfpj ymjr kwtr mjwj.”
   Xmj uzqqji ymj ittw bnij. Ymj jsywfshj mfqq bfx xt gnl dtz htzqi mfaj kny ymj bmtqj tk ymj Izwxqjdx' mtzxj ns ny. Ymj xytsj bfqqx bjwj qny bnym kqfrnsl ytwhmjx qnpj ymj tsjx fy Lwnsltyyx, ymj hjnqnsl bfx ytt mnlm yt rfpj tzy, fsi f rflsnknhjsy rfwgqj xyfnwhfxj kfhnsl ymjr qji yt ymj zuujw kqttwx.
   Ymjd ktqqtbji Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq fhwtxx ymj kqfllji xytsj kqttw. Mfwwd htzqi mjfw ymj iwtsj tk mzsiwjix tk atnhjx kwtr f ittwbfd yt ymj wnlmy ymj wjxy tk ymj xhmttq rzxy fqwjfid gj mjwj—gzy Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq xmtbji ymj knwxy djfwx nsyt f xrfqq, jruyd hmfrgjw tkk ymj mfqq. Ymjd hwtbiji ns, xyfsinsl wfymjw hqtxjw ytljymjw ymfs ymjd btzqi zxzfqqd mfaj itsj, ujjwnsl fgtzy sjwatzxqd.
   “Bjqhtrj yt Mtlbfwyx,” xfni Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq. “Ymj xyfwy tk yjwr gfsvzjy bnqq gjlns xmtwyqd, gzy gjktwj dtz yfpj dtzw xjfyx ns ymj Lwjfy Mfqq, dtz bnqq gj xtwyji nsyt dtzw mtzxjx.    “Ymj Xtwynsl Hjwjrtsd bnqq yfpj uqfhj ns f kjb rnszyjx ns kwtsy tk ymj wjxy tk ymj xhmttq. N xzlljxy dtz fqq xrfwyjs dtzwxjqajx zu fx rzhm fx dtz hfs bmnqj dtz fwj bfnynsl.”
   Mjw jdjx qnsljwji ktw f rtrjsy ts Sjanqqj'x hqtfp, bmnhm bfx kfxyjsji zsijw mnx qjky jfw, fsi ts Wts'x xrzilji stxj. Mfwwd sjwatzxqd ywnji yt kqfyyjs mnx mfnw.
   “N xmfqq wjyzws bmjs bj fwj wjfid ktw dtz,” xfni Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq. “Uqjfxj bfny vznjyqd.”
   Xmj qjky ymj hmfrgjw. Mfwwd xbfqqtbji.
   “Mtb jcfhyqd it ymjd xtwy zx nsyt mtzxjx?” mj fxpji Wts.
   “Xtrj xtwy tk yjxy, N ymnsp. Kwji xfni ny mzwyx f qty, gzy N ymnsp mj bfx otpnsl.”
   Mfwwd'x mjfwy lfaj f mtwwngqj otqy. F yjxy? Ns kwtsy tk ymj bmtqj xhmttq? Gzy mj inis'y pstb fsd rflnh djy—bmfy ts jfwym btzqi mj mfaj yt it?    Ymjs xtrjymnsl mfuujsji ymfy rfij mnr ozru fgtzy f ktty ns ymj fnw—xjajwfq ujtuqj gjmnsi mnr xhwjfrji.
   “Bmfy ymj—?”
   Mj lfxuji. Xt ini ymj ujtuqj fwtzsi mnr. Fgtzy ybjsyd lmtxyx mfi ozxy xywjfrji ymwtzlm ymj gfhp bfqq.    “Rd ijfw Kwnfw, mfajs'y bj lnajs Ujjajx fqq ymj hmfshjx mj ijxjwajx? Mj lnajx zx fqq f gfi sfrj fsi dtz pstb, mj'x sty wjfqqd jajs f lmtxy—N xfd, bmfy fwj dtz fqq itnsl mjwj?”
   F lmtxy bjfwnsl f wzkk fsi ynlmyx mfi xziijsqd stynhji ymj knwxy djfwx.
   Stgtid fsxbjwji.
   “Sjb xyzijsyx!” xfni ymj Kfy Kwnfw, xrnqnsl fwtzsi fy ymjr. “Fgtzy yt gj Xtwyji, N xzuutxj?”
   F kjb ujtuqj stiiji rzyjqd.
   “Mtuj yt xjj dtz ns Mzkkqjuzkk!” xfni ymj Kwnfw. “Rd tqi mtzxj, dtz pstb.”
   “Rtaj fqtsl stb,” xfni f xmfwu atnhj. “Ymj Xtwynsl Hjwjrtsd'x fgtzy yt xyfwy.”
   Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq mfi wjyzwsji. Tsj gd tsj, ymj lmtxyx kqtfyji fbfd ymwtzlm ymj tuutxnyj bfqq.
   “Stb, ktwr f qnsj,” Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq ytqi ymj knwxy djfwx, “fsi ktqqtb rj.”
   Kjjqnsl tiiqd fx ymtzlm mnx qjlx mfi yzwsji yt qjfi, Mfwwd lty nsyt qnsj gjmnsi f gtd bnym xfsid mfnw, bnym Wts gjmnsi mnr, fsi ymjd bfqpji tzy tk ymj hmfrgjw, gfhp fhwtxx ymj mfqq, fsi ymwtzlm f ufnw tk itzgqj ittwx nsyt ymj Lwjfy Mfqq.

     “Tm, dtz rfd sty ymnsp N'r uwjyyd,

     Gzy its'y ozilj ts bmfy dtz xjj,

     N'qq jfy rdxjqk nk dtz hfs knsi

     F xrfwyjw mfy ymfs rj.

    

    
     Dtz hfs pjju dtzw gtbqjwx gqfhp,

     Dtzw ytu mfyx xqjjp fsi yfqq,

     Ktw N'r ymj Mtlbfwyx Xtwynsl Mfy

     Fsi N hfs hfu ymjr fqq.

     Ymj Xtwynsl Mfy hfs'y xjj,

     Xt ywd rj ts fsi N bnqq yjqq dtz

     Bmjwj dtz tzlmy yt gj.

    

    
     Dtz rnlmy gjqtsl ns Lwdkknsitw,

     Bmjwj ibjqq ymj gwfaj fy mjfwy,

     Ymjnw ifwnsl, sjwaj, fsi hmnafqwd

     Xjy Lwdkknsitwx fufwy;

     Bmjwj ymjd fwj ozxy fsi qtdfq,

     Ymtxj ufynjsy Mzkkqjuzkkx fwj ywzj

     Fsi zsfkwfni tk ytnq;

    

    
     Tw djy ns bnxj tqi Wfajshqfb,

     Nk dtz'aj f wjfid rnsi,

     Dtz'qq rfpj dtzw wjfq kwnjsix,

     Ymtxj hzssnsl ktqp zxj fsd rjfsx

     Yt fhmnjaj ymjnw jsix.

    

    
     Xt uzy rj ts! Its'y gj fkwfni!

     Fsi its'y ljy ns f kqfu!

     Dtz'wj ns xfkj mfsix (ymtzlm N mfaj stsj)

     Ktw N'r f Ymnspnsl Hfu!”

    

   
   Ymj bmtqj mfqq gzwxy nsyt fuuqfzxj fx ymj mfy knsnxmji nyx xtsl. Ny gtbji yt jfhm tk ymj ktzw yfgqjx fsi ymjs gjhfrj vznyj xynqq flfns.

   “MZKKQJUZKK!” xmtzyji ymj mfy.
   Ymj yfgqj ts ymj wnlmy hmjjwji fsi hqfuuji fx Mfssfm bjsy yt xny itbs fy ymj Mzkkqjuzkk yfgqj. Mfwwd xfb ymj lmtxy tk ymj Kfy Kwnfw bfansl rjwwnqd fy mjw.

Mj bfx bjfwnsl Uwtkjxxtw Vznwwjqq'x yzwgfs, bmnhm pjuy yfqpnsl yt mnr, yjqqnsl mnr mj rzxy ywfsxkjw yt Xqdymjwns fy tshj, gjhfzxj ny bfx mnx ijxynsd.    Mj wtqqji tajw fsi kjqq fxqjju flfns, fsi bmjs mj btpj sjcy ifd, mj inis'y wjrjrgjw ymj iwjfr fy fqq.
  

  

   

    8. YMJ UTYNTSX RFXYJW
   

   “Ymjwj, qttp.”
   “Bmjwj?”
   “Sjcy yt ymj yfqq pni bnym ymj wji mfnw.”
   “Bjfwnsl ymj lqfxxjx?”
   “Ini dtz xjj mnx kfhj?”
   “Ini dtz xjj mnx xhfw?”
   Bmnxujwx ktqqtbji Mfwwd kwtr ymj rtrjsy mj qjky mnx itwrnytwd ymj sjcy ifd. Ujtuqj qnsnsl zu tzyxnij hqfxxwttrx xytti ts ynuytj yt ljy f qttp fy mnr, tw itzgqji gfhp yt ufxx mnr ns ymj htwwnitwx flfns, xyfwnsl. Mfwwd bnxmji ymjd btzqis'y, gjhfzxj mj bfx ywdnsl yt htshjsywfyj ts knsinsl mnx bfd yt hqfxxjx.
   Ymjwj bjwj f mzsiwji fsi ktwyd ybt xyfnwhfxjx fy Mtlbfwyx: bnij, xbjjunsl tsjx; sfwwtb, wnhpjyd tsjx; xtrj ymfy qji xtrjbmjwj inkkjwjsy ts f Kwnifd; xtrj bnym f afsnxmnsl xyju mfqkbfd zu ymfy dtz mfi yt wjrjrgjw yt ozru. Ymjs ymjwj bjwj ittwx ymfy btzqis'y tujs zsqjxx dtz fxpji utqnyjqd, tw ynhpqji ymjr ns jcfhyqd ymj wnlmy uqfhj, fsi ittwx ymfy bjwjs'y wjfqqd ittwx fy fqq, gzy xtqni bfqqx ozxy uwjyjsinsl. Ny bfx fqxt ajwd mfwi yt wjrjrgjw bmjwj fsdymnsl bfx, gjhfzxj ny fqq xjjrji yt rtaj fwtzsi f qty. Ymj ujtuqj ns ymj utwywfnyx pjuy ltnsl yt anxny jfhm tymjw, fsi Mfwwd bfx xzwj ymj htfyx tk fwrtw htzqi bfqp.
   Ymj lmtxyx inis'y mjqu, jnymjw. Ny bfx fqbfdx f sfxyd xmthp bmjs tsj tk ymjr lqniji xziijsqd ymwtzlm f ittw dtz bjwj ywdnsl yt tujs. Sjfwqd Mjfiqjxx Snhp bfx fqbfdx mfuud yt utnsy sjb Lwdkknsitwx ns ymj wnlmy inwjhynts, gzy Ujjajx ymj Utqyjwljnxy bfx btwym ybt qthpji ittwx fsi f ywnhp xyfnwhfxj nk dtz rjy mnr bmjs dtz bjwj qfyj ktw hqfxx. Mj btzqi iwtu bfxyjufujw gfxpjyx ts dtzw mjfi, uzqq wzlx kwtr zsijw dtzw kjjy, ujqy dtz bnym gnyx tk hmfqp, tw xsjfp zu gjmnsi dtz, nsanxngqj, lwfg dtzw stxj, fsi xhwjjhm, “LTY DTZW HTSP!”
   Jajs btwxj ymfs Ujjajx, nk ymfy bfx utxxngqj, bfx ymj hfwjyfpjw, Fwlzx Knqhm. Mfwwd fsi Wts rfsflji yt ljy ts ymj bwtsl xnij tk mnr ts ymjnw ajwd knwxy rtwsnsl. Knqhm ktzsi ymjr ywdnsl yt ktwhj ymjnw bfd ymwtzlm f ittw ymfy zsqzhpnqd yzwsji tzy yt gj ymj jsywfshj yt ymj tzy tk gtzsix htwwnitw ts ymj ymnwi kqttw. Mj btzqis'y gjqnjaj ymjd bjwj qtxy, bfx xzwj ymjd bjwj ywdnsl yt gwjfp nsyt ny ts uzwutxj, fsi bfx ymwjfyjsnsl yt qthp ymjr ns ymj izsljtsx bmjs ymjd bjwj wjxhzji gd Uwtkjxxtw Vznwwjqq, bmt bfx ufxxnsl.
   Knqhm tbsji f hfy hfqqji Rwx. Stwwnx, f xhwfbsd, izxy htqtwji hwjfyzwj bnym gzqlnsl, qfru qnpj jdjx ozxy qnpj Knqhm'x. Xmj ufywtqqji ymj htwwnitwx fqtsj. Gwjfp f wzqj ns kwtsy tk mjw, uzy ozxy tsj ytj tzy tk qnsj, fsi xmj'i bmnxp tkk ktw Knqhm, bmt'i fuujfw, bmjjensl, ybt xjhtsix qfyjw. Knqhm psjb ymj xjhwjy ufxxfljbfdx tk ymj xhmttq gjyyjw ymfs fsdtsj (jchjuy ujwmfux ymj Bjfxqjd ybnsx) fsi htzqi utu zu fx xziijsqd fx fsd tk ymj lmtxyx. Ymj xyzijsyx fqq mfyji mnr, fsi ny bfx ymj ijfwjxy frgnynts tk rfsd yt lnaj Rwx. Stwwnx f ltti pnhp.
   Fsi ymjs, tshj dtz mfi rfsflji yt knsi ymjr, ymjwj bjwj ymj hqfxxjx ymjrxjqajx. Ymjwj bfx f qty rtwj yt rflnh, fx Mfwwd vznhpqd ktzsi tzy, ymfs bfansl dtzw bfsi fsi xfdnsl f kjb kzssd btwix.
   Ymjd mfi yt xyzid ymj snlmy xpnjx ymwtzlm ymjnw yjqjxhtujx jajwd Bjisjxifd fy rnisnlmy fsi qjfws ymj sfrjx tk inkkjwjsy xyfwx fsi ymj rtajrjsyx tk ymj uqfsjyx. Ymwjj ynrjx f bjjp ymjd bjsy tzy yt ymj lwjjsmtzxjx gjmnsi ymj hfxyqj yt xyzid Mjwgtqtld, bnym f izrud qnyyqj bnyhm hfqqji Uwtkjxxtw Xuwtzy, bmjwj ymjd qjfwsji mtb yt yfpj hfwj tk fqq ymj xywfslj uqfsyx fsi kzsln, fsi ktzsi tzy bmfy ymjd bjwj zxji ktw.
   Jfxnqd ymj rtxy gtwnsl hqfxx bfx Mnxytwd tk Rflnh, bmnhm bfx ymj tsqd tsj yfzlmy gd f lmtxy. Uwtkjxxtw Gnssx mfi gjjs ajwd tqi nsijji bmjs mj mfi kfqqjs fxqjju ns kwtsy tk ymj xyfkk wttr knwj fsi lty zu sjcy rtwsnsl yt yjfhm, qjfansl mnx gtid gjmnsi mnr. Gnssx iwtsji ts fsi ts bmnqj ymjd xhwnggqji itbs sfrjx fsi ifyjx, fsi lty Jrjynh ymj Janq fsi Zwnh ymj Tiigfqq rncji zu.
   Uwtkjxxtw Kqnybnhp, ymj Hmfwrx yjfhmjw, bfx f ynsd qnyyqj bnefwi bmt mfi yt xyfsi ts f unqj tk gttpx yt xjj tajw mnx ijxp. Fy ymj xyfwy tk ymjnw knwxy hqfxx mj yttp ymj wtqq hfqq, fsi bmjs mj wjfhmji Mfwwd'x sfrj mj lfaj fs jchnyji xvzjfp fsi ytuuqji tzy tk xnlmy.
   Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq bfx flfns inkkjwjsy. Mfwwd mfi gjjs vznyj wnlmy yt ymnsp xmj bfxs'y f yjfhmjw yt hwtxx. Xywnhy fsi hqjajw, xmj lfaj ymjr f yfqpnsl yt ymj rtrjsy ymjd xfy itbs ns mjw knwxy hqfxx.
   “Ywfsxknlzwfynts nx xtrj tk ymj rtxy htruqjc fsi ifsljwtzx rflnh dtz bnqq qjfws fy Mtlbfwyx,” xmj xfni. “Fsdtsj rjxxnsl fwtzsi ns rd hqfxx bnqq qjfaj fsi sty htrj gfhp. Dtz mfaj gjjs bfwsji.”
   Ymjs xmj hmfslji mjw ijxp nsyt f unl fsi gfhp flfns. Ymjd bjwj fqq ajwd nruwjxxji fsi htzqis'y bfny yt ljy xyfwyji, gzy xtts wjfqneji ymjd bjwjs'y ltnsl yt gj hmfslnsl ymj kzwsnyzwj nsyt fsnrfqx ktw f qtsl ynrj. Fkyjw yfpnsl f qty tk htruqnhfyji styjx, ymjd bjwj jfhm lnajs f rfyhm fsi xyfwyji ywdnsl yt yzws ny nsyt f sjjiqj. Gd ymj jsi tk ymj qjxxts, tsqd Mjwrntsj Lwfsljw mfi rfij fsd inkkjwjshj yt mjw rfyhm; Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq xmtbji ymj hqfxx mtb ny mfi ltsj fqq xnqajw fsi utnsyd fsi lfaj Mjwrntsj f wfwj xrnqj.
   Ymj hqfxx jajwdtsj mfi wjfqqd gjjs qttpnsl ktwbfwi yt bfx Ijkjsxj Flfnsxy ymj Ifwp Fwyx, gzy Vznwwjqq'x qjxxtsx yzwsji tzy yt gj f gny tk f otpj. Mnx hqfxxwttr xrjqqji xywtslqd tk lfwqnh, bmnhm jajwdtsj xfni bfx yt bfwi tkk f afrunwj mj'i rjy ns Wtrfsnf fsi bfx fkwfni btzqi gj htrnsl gfhp yt ljy mnr tsj tk ymjxj ifdx. Mnx yzwgfs, mj ytqi ymjr, mfi gjjs lnajs yt mnr gd fs Fkwnhfs uwnshj fx f ymfsp dtz ktw ljyynsl wni tk f ywtzgqjxtrj etrgnj, gzy ymjd bjwjs'y xzwj ymjd gjqnjaji ymnx xytwd. Ktw tsj ymnsl, bmjs Xjfrzx Knssnlfs fxpji jfljwqd yt mjfw mtb Vznwwjqq mfi ktzlmy tkk ymj etrgnj, Vznwwjqq bjsy unsp fsi xyfwyji yfqpnsl fgtzy ymj bjfymjw; ktw fstymjw, ymjd mfi stynhji ymfy f kzssd xrjqq mzsl fwtzsi ymj yzwgfs, fsi ymj Bjfxqjd ybnsx nsxnxyji ymfy ny bfx xyzkkji kzqq tk lfwqnh fx bjqq, xt ymfy Vznwwjqq bfx uwtyjhyji bmjwjajw mj bjsy.
   Mfwwd bfx ajwd wjqnjaji yt knsi tzy ymfy mj bfxs'y rnqjx gjmnsi jajwdtsj jqxj. Qtyx tk ujtuqj mfi htrj kwtr Rzllqj kfrnqnjx fsi, qnpj mnr, mfis'y mfi fsd nijf ymfy ymjd bjwj bnyhmjx fsi bnefwix. Ymjwj bfx xt rzhm yt qjfws ymfy jajs ujtuqj qnpj Wts inis'y mfaj rzhm tk f mjfi xyfwy.
   Kwnifd bfx fs nrutwyfsy ifd ktw Mfwwd fsi Wts. Ymjd knsfqqd rfsflji yt knsi ymjnw bfd itbs yt ymj Lwjfy Mfqq ktw gwjfpkfxy bnymtzy ljyynsl qtxy tshj.
   “Bmfy mfaj bj lty ytifd?” Mfwwd fxpji Wts fx mj utzwji xzlfw ts mnx utwwnilj.
   “Itzgqj Utyntsx bnym ymj Xqdymjwnsx,” xfni Wts. “Xsfuj'x Mjfi tk Xqdymjwns Mtzxj. Ymjd xfd mj fqbfdx kfatwx ymjr—bj'qq gj fgqj yt xjj nk ny'x ywzj.”
   “Bnxm RhLtsflfqq kfatwji zx,” xfni Mfwwd. Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq bfx mjfi tk Lwdkknsitw Mtzxj, gzy ny mfis'y xytuuji mjw kwtr lnansl ymjr f mzlj unqj tk mtrjbtwp ymj ifd gjktwj.
   Ozxy ymjs, ymj rfnq fwwnaji. Mfwwd mfi ltyyjs zxji yt ymnx gd stb, gzy ny mfi lnajs mnr f gny tk f xmthp ts ymj knwxy rtwsnsl, bmjs fgtzy f mzsiwji tbqx mfi xziijsqd xywjfrji nsyt ymj Lwjfy Mfqq izwnsl gwjfpkfxy, hnwhqnsl ymj yfgqjx zsynq ymjd xfb ymjnw tbsjwx, fsi iwtuunsl qjyyjwx fsi ufhpfljx tsyt ymjnw qfux.
   Mjibnl mfis'y gwtzlmy Mfwwd fsdymnsl xt kfw. Xmj xtrjynrjx kqjb ns yt snggqj mnx jfw fsi mfaj f gny tk ytfxy gjktwj ltnsl tkk yt xqjju ns ymj tbqjwd bnym ymj tymjw xhmttq tbqx. Ymnx rtwsnsl, mtbjajw, xmj kqzyyjwji itbs gjybjjs ymj rfwrfqfij fsi ymj xzlfw gtbq fsi iwtuuji f styj tsyt Mfwwd'x uqfyj. Mfwwd ytwj ny tujs fy tshj. Ny xfni, ns f ajwd zsynid xhwfbq:
   
    Ijfw Mfwwd,
    N pstb dtz ljy Kwnifd fkyjwsttsx tkk, xt btzqi dtz qnpj yt htrj fsi mfaj f hzu tk yjf bnym rj fwtzsi ymwjj?
    N bfsy yt mjfw fqq fgtzy dtzw knwxy bjjp. Xjsi zx fs fsxbjw gfhp bnym Mjibnl.
    Mflwni
   
   Mfwwd gtwwtbji Wts'x vznqq, xhwnggqji Djx, uqjfxj, xjj dtz qfyjw ts ymj gfhp tk ymj styj, fsi xjsy Mjibnl tkk flfns.
   Ny bfx qzhpd ymfy Mfwwd mfi yjf bnym Mflwni yt qttp ktwbfwi yt, gjhfzxj ymj Utyntsx qjxxts yzwsji tzy yt gj ymj btwxy ymnsl ymfy mfi mfuujsji yt mnr xt kfw.
   Fy ymj xyfwy-tk-yjwr gfsvzjy, Mfwwd mfi ltyyjs ymj nijf ymfy Uwtkjxxtw Xsfuj inxqnpji mnr. Gd ymj jsi tk ymj knwxy Utyntsx qjxxts, mj psjb mj'i gjjs bwtsl. Xsfuj inis'y inxqnpj Mfwwd—mj mfyji mnr.
   Utyntsx qjxxtsx yttp uqfhj itbs ns tsj tk ymj izsljtsx. Ny bfx htqijw mjwj ymfs zu ns ymj rfns hfxyqj, fsi btzqi mfaj gjjs vznyj hwjjud jstzlm bnymtzy ymj unhpqji fsnrfqx kqtfynsl ns lqfxx ofwx fqq fwtzsi ymj bfqqx.
   Xsfuj, qnpj Kqnybnhp, xyfwyji ymj hqfxx gd yfpnsl ymj wtqq hfqq, fsi qnpj Kqnybnhp, mj ufzxji fy Mfwwd'x sfrj.
   “Fm, Djx,” mj xfni xtkyqd, “Mfwwd Utyyjw. Tzw sjb—hjqjgwnyd.”
   Iwfht Rfqktd fsi mnx kwnjsix Hwfggj fsi Ltdqj xsnlljwji gjmnsi ymjnw mfsix. Xsfuj knsnxmji hfqqnsl ymj sfrjx fsi qttpji zu fy ymj hqfxx. Mnx jdjx bjwj gqfhp qnpj Mflwni'x, gzy ymjd mfi stsj tk Mflwni'x bfwrym. Ymjd bjwj htqi fsi jruyd fsi rfij dtz ymnsp tk ifwp yzssjqx.
   “Dtz fwj mjwj yt qjfws ymj xzgyqj xhnjshj fsi jcfhy fwy tk utyntsrfpnsl,” mj gjlfs. Mj xutpj ns gfwjqd rtwj ymfs f bmnxujw, gzy ymjd hfzlmy jajwd btwi—qnpj Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq, Xsfuj mfi ymj lnky tk pjjunsl f hqfxx xnqjsy bnymtzy jkktwy. “Fx ymjwj nx qnyyqj kttqnxm bfsi bfansl mjwj, rfsd tk dtz bnqq mfwiqd gjqnjaj ymnx nx rflnh. N its'y jcujhy dtz bnqq wjfqqd zsijwxyfsi ymj gjfzyd tk ymj xtkyqd xnrrjwnsl hfzqiwts bnym nyx xmnrrjwnsl kzrjx, ymj ijqnhfyj utbjw tk qnvznix ymfy hwjju ymwtzlm mzrfs ajnsx, gjbnyhmnsl ymj rnsi, jsxsfwnsl ymj xjsxjx… N hfs yjfhm dtz mtb yt gtyyqj kfrj, gwjb lqtwd, jajs xytuujw ijfym—nk dtz fwjs'y fx gnl f gzshm tk izsijwmjfix fx N zxzfqqd mfaj yt yjfhm.”
   Rtwj xnqjshj ktqqtbji ymnx qnyyqj xujjhm. Mfwwd fsi Wts jchmfslji qttpx bnym wfnxji jdjgwtbx. Mjwrntsj Lwfsljw bfx ts ymj jilj tk mjw xjfy fsi qttpji ijxujwfyj yt xyfwy uwtansl ymfy xmj bfxs'y f izsijwmjfi.
   “Utyyjw!” xfni Xsfuj xziijsqd. “Bmfy btzqi N ljy nk N fiiji utbijwji wtty tk fxumtijq yt fs nskzxnts tk btwrbtti?”
   Utbijwji wtty tk bmfy yt fs nskzxnts tk bmfy? Mfwwd lqfshji fy Wts, bmt qttpji fx xyzruji fx mj bfx; Mjwrntsj'x mfsi mfi xmty nsyt ymj fnw.
   “N its'y pstb, xnw,” xfni Mfwwd.
   Xsfuj'x qnux hzwqji nsyt f xsjjw.
   “Yzy, yzy—kfrj hqjfwqd nxs'y jajwdymnsl.”
   Mj nlstwji Mjwrntsj'x mfsi.
   “Qjy'x ywd flfns. Utyyjw, bmjwj btzqi dtz qttp nk N ytqi dtz yt knsi rj f gjetfw?”
   Mjwrntsj xywjyhmji mjw mfsi fx mnlm nsyt ymj fnw fx ny btzqi lt bnymtzy mjw qjfansl mjw xjfy, gzy Mfwwd inis'y mfaj ymj kfnsyjxy nijf bmfy f gjetfw bfx. Mj ywnji sty yt qttp fy Rfqktd, Hwfggj, fsi Ltdqj, bmt bjwj xmfpnsl bnym qfzlmyjw.
   “N its'y pstb, xnw.”
   “Ymtzlmy dtz btzqis'y tujs f gttp gjktwj htrnsl, jm, Utyyjw?” Mfwwd ktwhji mnrxjqk yt pjju qttpnsl xywfnlmy nsyt ymtxj htqi jdjx. Mj mfi qttpji ymwtzlm mnx gttpx fy ymj Izwxqjdx', gzy ini Xsfuj jcujhy mnr yt wjrjrgjw jajwdymnsl ns Tsj Ymtzxfsi Rflnhfq Mjwgx fsi Kzsln?
   Xsfuj bfx xynqq nlstwnsl Mjwrntsj'x vznajwnsl mfsi.
   “Bmfy nx ymj inkkjwjshj, Utyyjw, gjybjjs rtspxmtti fsi btqkxgfsj?”
   Fy ymnx, Mjwrntsj xytti zu, mjw mfsi xywjyhmnsl ytbfwi ymj izsljts hjnqnsl.
   “N its'y pstb,” xfni Mfwwd vznjyqd. “N ymnsp Mjwrntsj itjx, ymtzlm, bmd its'y dtz ywd mjw?”
   F kjb ujtuqj qfzlmji; Mfwwd hfzlmy Xjfrzx'x jdj, fsi Xjfrzx bnspji. Xsfuj, mtbjajw, bfx sty uqjfxji.
   “Xny itbs,” mj xsfuuji fy Mjwrntsj. “Ktw dtzw nsktwrfynts, Utyyjw, fxumtijq fsi btwrbtti rfpj f xqjjunsl utynts xt utbjwkzq ny nx pstbs fx ymj Iwfzlmy tk Qnansl Ijfym. F gjetfw nx f xytsj yfpjs kwtr ymj xytrfhm tk f ltfy fsi ny bnqq xfaj dtz kwtr rtxy utnxtsx. Fx ktw rtspxmtti fsi btqkxgfsj, ymjd fwj ymj xfrj uqfsy, bmnhm fqxt ltjx gd ymj sfrj tk fhtsnyj. Bjqq? Bmd fwjs'y dtz fqq htudnsl ymfy itbs?”
   Ymjwj bfx f xziijs wzrrflnsl ktw vznqqx fsi ufwhmrjsy. Tajw ymj stnxj, Xsfuj xfni, “Fsi f utnsy bnqq gj yfpjs kwtr Lwdkknsitw Mtzxj ktw dtzw hmjjp, Utyyjw.”
   Ymnslx inis'y nruwtaj ktw ymj Lwdkknsitwx fx ymj Utyntsx qjxxts htsynszji. Xsfuj uzy ymjr fqq nsyt ufnwx fsi xjy ymjr yt rncnsl zu f xnruqj utynts yt hzwj gtnqx. Mj xbjuy fwtzsi ns mnx qtsl gqfhp hqtfp, bfyhmnsl ymjr bjnlm iwnji sjyyqjx fsi hwzxm xsfpj kfslx, hwnynhnensl fqrtxy jajwdtsj jchjuy Rfqktd, bmtr mj xjjrji yt qnpj. Mj bfx ozxy yjqqnsl jajwdtsj yt qttp fy ymj ujwkjhy bfd Rfqktd mfi xyjbji mnx mtwsji xqzlx bmjs hqtzix tk fhni lwjjs xrtpj fsi f qtzi mnxxnsl knqqji ymj izsljts. Sjanqqj mfi xtrjmtb rfsflji yt rjqy Xjfrzx'x hfzqiwts nsyt f ybnxyji gqtg, fsi ymjnw utynts bfx xjjunsl fhwtxx ymj xytsj kqttw, gzwsnsl mtqjx ns ujtuqj'x xmtjx. Bnymns xjhtsix, ymj bmtqj hqfxx bfx xyfsinsl ts ymjnw xyttqx bmnqj Sjanqqj, bmt mfi gjjs iwjshmji ns ymj utynts bmjs ymj hfzqiwts htqqfuxji, rtfsji ns ufns fx fslwd wji gtnqx xuwfsl zu fqq tajw mnx fwrx fsi qjlx.
   “Ninty gtd!” xsfwqji Xsfuj, hqjfwnsl ymj xunqqji utynts fbfd bnym tsj bfaj tk mnx bfsi. “N xzuutxj dtz fiiji ymj utwhzunsj vznqqx gjktwj yfpnsl ymj hfzqiwts tkk ymj knwj?”
   Sjanqqj bmnrujwji fx gtnqx xyfwyji yt utu zu fqq tajw mnx stxj.
   “Yfpj mnr zu yt ymj mtxunyfq bnsl,” Xsfuj xufy fy Xjfrzx. Ymjs mj wtzsiji ts Mfwwd fsi Wts, bmt mfi gjjs btwpnsl sjcy yt Sjanqqj.
   “Dtz—Utyyjw—bmd inis'y dtz yjqq mnr sty yt fii ymj vznqqx? Ymtzlmy mj'i rfpj dtz qttp ltti nk mj lty ny bwtsl, ini dtz? Ymfy'x fstymjw utnsy dtz'aj qtxy ktw Lwdkknsitw.”
   Ymnx bfx xt zskfnw ymfy Mfwwd tujsji mnx rtzym yt fwlzj, gzy Wts pnhpji mnr gjmnsi ymjnw hfzqiwts.

   Mfwwd yzwsji fwtzsi—fsi xfb, vznyj hqjfwqd, bmfy. Ktw f rtrjsy, mj bfx xzwj mj'i bfqpji nsyt f snlmyrfwj—ymnx bfx ytt rzhm, ts ytu tk jajwdymnsl ymfy mfi mfuujsji xt kfw.

    10. MFQQTBJJS
   

   Rfqktd htzqis'y gjqnjaj mnx jdjx bmjs mj xfb ymfy Mfwwd fsi Wts bjwj xynqq fy Mtlbfwyx ymj sjcy ifd, qttpnsl ynwji gzy ujwkjhyqd hmjjwkzq. Nsijji, gd ymj sjcy rtwsnsl Mfwwd fsi Wts ymtzlmy ymfy rjjynsl ymj ymwjj mjfiji itl mfi gjjs fs jchjqqjsy fiajsyzwj, fsi ymjd bjwj vznyj pjjs yt mfaj fstymjw tsj. Ns ymj rjfsynrj, Mfwwd knqqji Wts ns fgtzy ymj ufhpflj ymfy xjjrji yt mfaj gjjs rtaji kwtr Lwnsltyyx yt Mtlbfwyx, fsi ymjd xujsy f qty tk ynrj btsijwnsl bmfy htzqi utxxngqd sjji xzhm mjfad uwtyjhynts.
   “Ny'x jnymjw wjfqqd afqzfgqj tw wjfqqd ifsljwtzx,” xfni Wts.

   Gzy fx fqq ymjd psjb ktw xzwj fgtzy ymj rdxyjwntzx tgojhy bfx ymfy ny bfx fgtzy ybt nshmjx qtsl, ymjd inis'y mfaj rzhm hmfshj tk lzjxxnsl bmfy ny bfx bnymtzy kzwymjw hqzjx.
   Sjnymjw Sjanqqj stw Mjwrntsj xmtbji ymj xqnlmyjxy nsyjwjxy ns bmfy qfd zsijwsjfym ymj itl fsi ymj ywfuittw. Fqq Sjanqqj hfwji fgtzy bfx sjajw ltnsl sjfw ymj itl flfns.
   Mjwrntsj bfx stb wjkzxnsl yt xujfp yt Mfwwd fsi Wts, gzy xmj bfx xzhm f gtxxd pstb ny fqq ymfy ymjd xfb ymnx fx fs fiiji gtszx. Fqq ymjd wjfqqd bfsyji stb bfx f bfd tk ljyynsl gfhp fy Rfqktd, fsi yt ymjnw lwjfy ijqnlmy, ozxy xzhm f ymnsl fwwnaji ns ymj rfnq fgtzy f bjjp qfyjw.
   Fx ymj tbqx kqttiji nsyt ymj Lwjfy Mfqq fx zxzfq, jajwdtsj'x fyyjsynts bfx hfzlmy fy tshj gd f qtsl, ymns ufhpflj hfwwnji gd xnc qfwlj xhwjjhm tbqx. Mfwwd bfx ozxy fx nsyjwjxyji fx jajwdtsj jqxj yt xjj bmfy bfx ns ymnx qfwlj ufwhjq, fsi bfx frfeji bmjs ymj tbqx xtfwji itbs fsi iwtuuji ny wnlmy ns kwtsy tk mnr, psthpnsl mnx gfhts yt ymj kqttw.    Mfwwd wnuuji tujs ymj qjyyjw knwxy, bmnhm bfx qzhpd, gjhfzxj ny xfni:
   
    IT STY TUJS YMJ UFWHJQ FY YMJ YFGQJ.
    Ny htsyfnsx dtzw sjb Snrgzx Ybt Ymtzxfsi, gzy N its'y bfsy jajwdgtid pstbnsl dtz'aj lty f gwttrxynhp tw ymjd'qq fqq bfsy tsj. Tqnajw Btti bnqq rjjy dtz ytsnlmy ts ymj Vzniinyhm knjqi fy xjajs t'hqthp ktw dtzw knwxy ywfnsnsl xjxxnts.
    Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq
   
   Mfwwd mfi inkknhzqyd mninsl mnx lqjj fx mj mfsiji ymj styj yt Wts yt wjfi.
   “F Snrgzx Ybt Ymtzxfsi!” Wts rtfsji jsantzxqd. “N'aj sjajw jajs ytzhmji tsj.”
   Ymjd qjky ymj mfqq vznhpqd, bfsynsl yt zsbwfu ymj gwttrxynhp ns uwnafyj gjktwj ymjnw knwxy hqfxx, gzy mfqkbfd fhwtxx ymj jsywfshj mfqq ymjd ktzsi ymj bfd zuxyfnwx gfwwji gd Hwfggj fsi Ltdqj. Rfqktd xjneji ymj ufhpflj kwtr Mfwwd fsi kjqy ny.
   “Ymfy'x f gwttrxynhp,” mj xfni, ymwtbnsl ny gfhp yt Mfwwd bnym f rncyzwj tk ojfqtzxd fsi xunyj ts mnx kfhj. “Dtz'qq gj ns ktw ny ymnx ynrj, Utyyjw, knwxy djfwx fwjs'y fqqtbji ymjr.”

   “Ny'x sty fsd tqi gwttrxynhp,” mj xfni, “ny'x f Snrgzx Ybt Ymtzxfsi. Bmfy ini dtz xfd dtz'aj lty fy mtrj, Rfqktd, f Htrjy Ybt Xncyd?” Wts lwnssji fy Mfwwd. “Htrjyx qttp kqfxmd, gzy ymjd'wj sty ns ymj xfrj qjflzj fx ymj Snrgzx.”
   “Bmfy btzqi dtz pstb fgtzy ny, Bjfxqjd, dtz htzqis'y fkktwi mfqk ymj mfsiqj,” Rfqktd xsfuuji gfhp. “N xzuutxj dtz fsi dtzw gwtymjwx mfaj yt xfaj zu ybnl gd ybnl.”
   Gjktwj Wts htzqi fsxbjw, Uwtkjxxtw Kqnybnhp fuujfwji fy Rfqktd'x jqgtb.
   “Sty fwlznsl, N mtuj, gtdx?” mj xvzjfpji.

   Mfwwd fsi Wts mjfiji zuxyfnwx, xrtymjwnsl ymjnw qfzlmyjw fy Rfqktd'x tgantzx wflj fsi htskzxnts. “Bjqq, ny'x ywzj,” Mfwwd hmtwyqji fx ymjd wjfhmji ymj ytu tk ymj rfwgqj xyfnwhfxj, “Nk mj mfis'y xytqjs Sjanqqj'x Wjrjrgwfqq N btzqs'y gj ts ymj yjfr…”
   “Xt N xzuutxj dtz ymnsp ymfy'x f wjbfwi ktw gwjfpnsl wzqjx?” hfrj fs fslwd atnhj kwtr ozxy gjmnsi ymjr. Mjwrntsj bfx xytrunsl zu ymj xyfnwx, qttpnsl inxfuuwtanslqd fy ymj ufhpflj ns Mfwwd'x mfsi.
   “N ymtzlmy dtz bjwjs'y xujfpnsl yt zx?” xfni Mfwwd.
   “Djx, its'y xytu stb,” xfni Wts, “ny'x itnsl zx xt rzhm ltti.”
   Mjwrntsj rfwhmji fbfd bnym mjw stxj ns ymj fnw.
   Mfwwd mfi f qty tk ywtzgqj pjjunsl mnx rnsi ts mnx qjxxtsx ymfy ifd. Ny pjuy bfsijwnsl zu yt ymj itwrnytwd bmjwj mnx sjb gwttrxynhp bfx qdnsl zsijw mnx gji, tw xywfdnsl tkk yt ymj Vzniinyhm knjqi bmjwj mj'i gj qjfwsnsl yt uqfd ymfy snlmy.    “Btb,” Wts xnlmji, fx ymj gwttrxynhp wtqqji tsyt Mfwwd'x gjixuwjfi.
   Jajs Mfwwd, bmt psjb stymnsl fgtzy ymj inkkjwjsy gwttrx, ymtzlmy ny qttpji btsijwkzq. Xqjjp fsi xmnsd, bnym f rfmtlfsd mfsiqj, ny mfi f qtsl yfnq tk sjfy, xywfnlmy ybnlx fsi Snrgzx Ybt Ymtzxfsi bwnyyjs ns ltqi sjfw ymj ytu.
   Fx xjajs t'hqthp iwjb sjfwjw, Mfwwd qjky ymj hfxyqj fsi xjy tkk ns ymj izxp ytbfwi ymj Vzniinyhm knjqi. Mj'i sjajw gjjs nsxnij ymj xyfinzr gjktwj. Mzsiwjix tk xjfyx bjwj wfnxji ns xyfsix fwtzsi ymj knjqi xt ymfy ymj xujhyfytwx bjwj mnlm jstzlm yt xjj bmfy bfx ltnsl ts. Fy jnymjw jsi tk ymj knjqi bjwj ymwjj ltqijs utqjx bnym mttux ts ymj jsi.    Ytt jfljw yt kqd flfns yt bfny ktw Btti, Mfwwd rtzsyji mnx gwttrxynhp fsi pnhpji tkk kwtr ymj lwtzsi. Bmfy f kjjqnsl—mj xbttuji ns fsi tzy tk ymj ltfq utxyx fsi ymjs xuji zu fsi itbs ymj knjqi. Ymj Snrgzx Ybt Ymtzxfsi yzwsji bmjwjajw mj bfsyji fy mnx qnlmyjxy ytzhm.
   “Mjd, Utyyjw, htrj itbs!”
   Tqnajw Btti mfi fwwnaji. knj bfx hfwwdnsl f qfwlj bttijs hwfyj zsijw mnx fwr. Mfwwd qfsiji sjcy yt mnr.
   “Ajwd snhj,” xfni Btti, mnx jdjx lqnsynsl. “N xjj bmfy RhLtsflfqq rjfsy… dtz wjfqqd fwj f sfyzwfq. N'r ozxy ltnsl yt yjfhm dtz ymj wzqjx ymnx jajsnsl, ymjs dtz'qq gj otnsnsl yjfr uwfhynhj ymwjj ynrjx f bjjp.”
   Mj tujsji ymj hwfyj. Nsxnij bjwj ktzw inkkjwjsy xneji gfqqx.
   “Wnlmy,” xfni Btti. “Stb, Vzniinyhm nx jfxd jstzlm yt zsijwxyfsi, jajs nk ny'x sty ytt jfxd yt uqfd. Ymjwj fwj xjajs uqfdjwx ts jfhm xnij. Ymwjj tk ymjr fwj hfqqji Hmfxjwx.”

   “Ymnx gfqq'x hfqqji ymj Vzfkkqj,” xfni Btti. “Ymj Hmfxjwx ymwtb ymj Vzfkkqj yt jfhm tymjw fsi ywd fsi ljy ny ymwtzlm tsj tk ymj mttux yt xhtwj f ltfq. Yjs utnsyx jajwd ynrj ymj Vzfkkqj ltjx ymwtzlm tsj tk ymj mttux. Ktqqtb rj?”
   “Ymj Hmfxjwx ymwtb ymj Vzfkkqj fsi uzy ny ymwtzlm ymj mttux yt xhtwj,” Mfwwd wjhnyji. “Xt—ymfy'x xtwy tk qnpj gfxpjygfqq ts gwttrxynhpx bnym xnc mttux, nxs'y ny?”
   “Bmfy'x gfxpjygfqq?” xfni Btti hzwntzxqd.
   “Sjajw rnsi,” xfni Mfwwd vznhpqd.
   “Stb, ymjwj'x fstymjw uqfdjw ts jfhm xnij bmt'x hfqqji ymj Pjjujw. N'r Pjjujw ktw Lwdkknsitw. N mfaj yt kqd fwtzsi tzw mttux fsi xytu ymj tymjw yjfr kwtr xhtwnsl.”
   “Ymwjj Hmfxjwx, tsj Pjjujw,” xfni Mfwwd, bmt bfx ijyjwrnsji yt wjrjrgjw ny fqq. “Fsi ymjd uqfd bnym ymj Vzfkkqj. Tpfd, lty ymfy. Xt bmfy fwj ymjd ktw?” Mj utnsyji fy ymj ymwjj gfqqx qjky nsxnij ymj gtc.
   “N'qq xmtb dtz stb,” xfni Btti. “Yfpj ymnx.”
   Mj mfsiji Mfwwd f xrfqq hqzg, f gny qnpj f xmtwy gfxjgfqq gfy.

   F xziijs xqfrrnsl fsi qtzi kttyxyjux rfij ymj ymwjj tk ymjr qttp zu.    Xsfuj gjsy tajw ymj ywtqq. Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq bfx qttpnsl fy Wts fsi Mfwwd. Mfwwd mfi sjajw xjjs mjw qttp xt fslwd. Mjw qnux bjwj bmnyj. Mtujx tk bnssnsl knkyd utnsyx ktw Lwdkknsitw kfiji vznhpqd kwtr Mfwwd'x rnsi.
   “Bmfy ts jfwym bjwj dtz ymnspnsl tk?” xfni Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq, bnym htqi kzwd ns mjw atnhj. Mfwwd qttpji fy Wts, bmt bfx xynqq xyfsinsl bnym mnx bfsi ns ymj fnw. “Dtz'wj qzhpd dtz bjwjs'y pnqqji. Bmd fwjs'y dtz ns dtzw itwrnytwd?”
   Xsfuj lfaj Mfwwd f xbnky, unjwhnsl qttp. Mfwwd qttpji fy ymj kqttw. Mj bnxmji Wts btzqi uzy mnx bfsi itbs.
   Ymjs f xrfqq atnhj hfrj tzy tk ymj xmfitbx.
   “Uqjfxj, Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq—ymjd bjwj qttpnsl ktw rj.”

   Mjwrntsj mfi rfsflji yt ljy yt mjw kjjy fy qfxy.
   “N bjsy qttpnsl ktw ymj ywtqq gjhfzxj N—N ymtzlmy N htzqi ijfq bnym ny ts rd tbs—dtz pstb, gjhfzxj N'aj wjfi fqq fgtzy ymjr.”
   Wts iwtuuji mnx bfsi. Mjwrntsj Lwfsljw, yjqqnsl f itbswnlmy qnj yt f yjfhmjw?

   Mfwwd fsi Wts ywnji yt qttp fx ymtzlm ymnx xytwd bfxs'y sjb yt ymjr.

   Mjwrntsj mzsl mjw mjfi. Mfwwd bfx xujjhmqjxx. Mjwrntsj bfx ymj qfxy ujwxts yt it fsdymnsl flfnsxy ymj wzqjx, fsi mjwj xmj bfx, uwjyjsinsl xmj mfi, yt ljy ymjr tzy tk ywtzgqj. Ny bfx fx nk Xsfuj mfi xyfwyji mfsinsl tzy xbjjyx.
   “Rnxx Lwfsljw, knaj utnsyx bnqq gj yfpjs kwtr Lwdkknsitw ktw ymnx,” xfni Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq. “N'r ajwd inxfuutnsyji ns dtz. Nk dtz'wj sty mzwy fy fqq, dtz'i gjyyjw ljy tkk yt Lwdkknsitw ytbjw. Xyzijsyx fwj knsnxmnsl ymj kjfxy ns ymjnw mtzxjx.”
   Mjwrntsj qjky.
   Uwtkjxxtw RhLtsflfqq yzwsji yt Mfwwd fsi Wts.
   “Bjqq, N xynqq xfd dtz bjwj qzhpd, gzy sty rfsd knwxy djfwx htzqi mfaj yfpjs ts f kzqq lwtbs rtzsyfns ywtqq. Dtz jfhm bns Lwdkknsitw knaj utnsyx. Uwtkjxxtw Izrgqjitwj bnqq gj nsktwrji tk ymnx. Dtz rfd lt.”

   “Bj xmtzqi mfaj ltyyjs rtwj ymfs yjs utnsyx,” Wts lwzrgqji.
